Ministry of Interior's Opinions on the Provincial Governor System 43

(Nanjing) Regarding the issue of changing to a provincial governor system, the Central Political Council handed it over to the Executive Yuan to solicit opinions from relevant departments. The Ministry of Interior believes that the provincial governor system should have been implemented long ago to realize the separation of military and civilian affairs. They have drafted the following points to note when changing to a provincial governor system: (1) Establishing something similar to the previous provincial assemblies, or calling them provincial political councils; (2) The various departments are concentrated and the governor is busy with affairs, so he cannot take care of everything. A Department of Political Affairs (or other) should be established to assist in handling provincial affairs, etc., to improve the organization in order to achieve perfection and avoid malpractices. This will be reported to the Executive Yuan, requesting that it be implemented immediately. (28th Dispatch)

Ministry of Industry Plans to Operate Ammonium Sulfate Plant Independently 44

(Nanjing) The draft contract for the Sino-British-German joint venture ammonium sulfate plant has expired. Because the conditions of the British Brunner Mond Company and the German IG Farben Company were very harsh, it has been terminated. The Ministry of Industry plans to operate it independently, reducing the capital from 15 million to 7 million yuan, and requesting the Executive Yuan to allocate 7 million yuan from the American cotton and wheat loan. It is still awaiting approval from the Executive Yuan. As for the plant site, because ammonium sulfate is related to the steel plant, it would be most appropriate to build them together near Ma'anshan. (28th Dispatch)

Chairman Chiang Inspects Military Situation at the Front 45

High Morale of the Bandit Suppression Troops

(Nanchang) There are a large number of Central Army troops currently gathered in the northern Jiangxi area. At the same time, Chiang's return here indicates that a large-scale bandit suppression operation will soon be implemented. Everyone here expects that Chiang is determined to win this time. Chiang's guard team, which has been trained by German instructors for a long time, recently arrived here from Nanjing. All the equipment is excellent and the uniforms are neat. After Chiang arrived here, the soldiers and officers of the various armies were greatly encouraged and worked hard. Airfields have been built along the Yushan Railway. The large airfield in Nanchang has 30,000 workers working day and night to repair it. On the 25th of this month, Chiang issued a handwritten order limiting the completion of the airfield to the end of this month. Therefore, Jiangxi Chairman Xiong Shihui personally supervised the construction to encourage the workers and allocated 10,000 yuan as a reward for the workers. Next week, the completion ceremony of the airfield will be held. At that time, many aircraft will fly in the sky over Nanchang and then fly to the front lines to participate in the bandit suppression operation. Recently, transport coolies recruited from the inland have been transported to Jiujiang one after another. Among them, people from Zhejiang, Shandong, Henan, Jiangsu, and Anhui provinces are the most numerous. (29th Reuters Telegram)

Page 6

Eloquent Debates Commence at League of Nations Assembly 49

Anti-German Sentiment Runs High

Simon Supports the League of Nations and Disarmament

Austrian Chancellor's Speech Applauded by the Entire Audience

Germany's Position Falls into Isolation

(Geneva) British Foreign Secretary Simon spoke at the League of Nations Assembly today, vigorously defending the League of Nations and the Disarmament Conference, and pointing out that others' criticisms were unfair. Simon's words were clearly directed at Norwegian Prime Minister Mowinckel's remarks yesterday that the League of Nations and the Disarmament Conference had not made progress. Simon strongly urged all countries in the world to achieve results in disarmament as soon as possible, saying that if disarmament is achieved, its power to promote economic recovery will be greater than anything else. Simon suggested that the existing draft disarmament treaty be slightly revised, which would facilitate the formulation of a gradual disarmament plan. Simon continued, saying that the League of Nations has a special responsibility under the treaties protecting minorities, and must guarantee fair treatment for minorities who differ in religion, race, and language from the majority rulers. When Simon made this statement, he looked at German delegate Dr. Goebbels. Whether Simon did this intentionally or unintentionally, the audience spoke highly of it. When Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss rose to speak, the entire audience applauded, except for the German delegation. This kind of expression is rare. The Austrian Chancellor spoke cautiously and self-restrainedly, only speaking about the difficult economic situation in Austria. (27th Reuters Telegram)

Simon Describes Disarmament Steps 50

(Geneva) The League of Nations Assembly's open debate began this afternoon. British representative Simon spoke first. Simon first said that the League of Nations' work has been of great value with the cooperation of the United States. He asserted that economic recovery has begun to show signs in recent months, but it can only be hoped to be completed quickly after the disarmament issue is resolved. Simon later said that recently, major powers have been blamed, saying that disarmament is not only a matter between a few major powers, but that all member states of the League of Nations are actually concerned about this matter. However, it must be known that major powers not only have a very great responsibility, but also bear the greatest burden. Therefore, a preliminary understanding must be established between the major powers. The purpose of the major powers gathering again for consultations is that although the British disarmament plan has been accepted by all countries as the basis for discussion, there are still other obstacles ahead, and now we have to find ways to eliminate them. Moreover, the countries now deeply feel the difficulty of the road ahead. No matter how important, the first goal of the Disarmament Conference, that is, the most important goal, should at least be to establish an arms treaty. In this way, the coordination of the first step in disarmament can be established, and the subsequent paragraphs will be easier to achieve. Simon did not say that the security issue is too complicated, and he cannot discuss it now, but if countries can strive for self-improvement in the spirit of good neighborliness, then general trust will be greatly consolidated.

League of Nations Protects Minorities 51

(Geneva) Simon's speech continued to address the issue of minorities, saying that this is one of the most important tasks of the League of Nations Council, and the majority ruling nation should give fair treatment to minorities of different races, languages, and religions. Simon dispelled the doubts held outside on the disarmament issue, saying that anyone who criticizes the slow progress of the Disarmament Conference disregards the various difficulties encountered by the conference. It should be known that this cannot be blamed on one country. Now that the technical issues have been thoroughly discussed, it is urgent to quickly sign an arms convention so that clear results can be obtained.

Austria Determined to Maintain Independence 52

After Simon's speech, everyone applauded in approval. Then Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss took the stage to speak, and was also welcomed by the audience. Dollfuss said that now is not the time for countries to protect themselves, but also to consider that outside the borders, there are still living beings who are also flesh and blood. Austria is now preparing to adopt a new constitution based on the principles announced by the Pope. Recently, at the Catholic Congress held in Vienna, the Austrian people expressed their devout belief in Catholicism. In a firm tone, Dollfuss announced Austria's determination to maintain its independence. Then Canadian representative Mennivock passionately advocated the rationalization of the arms industry. Then Chairman Walther announced the adjournment of the meeting until Friday, apparently because only a few people had registered to speak. Now it is hoped that more representatives will register to speak so that the conference can have more vitality in the discussion. (27th National Telegram)

French and German Foreign Ministers Meet for the First Time 53

(Geneva) The representatives of various countries attending the League of Nations Assembly had many talks today. For example, French Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour met with Italian representative Aloisi and Soviet representative Litvinov one after another, and then talked with British Foreign Secretary Simon. In addition, Polish Foreign Minister Beck met with US representative Davis at the Disarmament Conference and Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss. Also, when the Assistant Secretary of the League of Nations, the German Torrent Lamb, hosted a banquet tonight, French Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour will meet with German Foreign Minister Neurath. (28th Havas Telegram)

The Little Entente Countries Decide on a United Front 54

Treaty Cannot Be Modified

Advocating the Implementation of Sanctions

Capital of Romania The Little Entente countries issued a communique after holding their last meeting in Sinaia. It stated that the foreign ministers of Romania, Czechoslovakia, and Yugoslavia have completely consistent views on the overall political and financial situation in Europe. Although improvements have been seen in some aspects, the situation is still serious in some places. The three foreign ministers were quite satisfied with the non-aggression treaties signed between the Soviet Union and various countries, but they believed that the situation in Central Europe was quite worrying. The three foreign ministers also decided on the policy that should be adopted when discussing Central European issues internationally, that is, on the one hand, insisting that the peace treaties cannot be modified, and on the other hand, advocating economic cooperation with neighboring countries. The three foreign ministers also elaborated on the economic plan set by the Little Entente countries when they met in Prague in June of this year and adopted various decisions to make it a concrete plan and strive to realize it in the short term. The economic conference of the Little Entente countries is scheduled to be convened at the beginning of November this year. Regarding the issue of disarmament, the Little Entente countries advocated supporting all countries in their efforts to realize general peace and enabling the automatic and effective arms inspection system to be implemented uniformly in all countries. They also advocated that sanctions must be tried to prevent countries from violating the arms convention that is about to be signed. Also, the two non-aggression treaties signed by Romania and its neighboring countries and the Soviet Union one after another on July 3 and 4 of this year have been approved by King Carol and all outstanding issues between Romania and Yugoslavia have been resolved. (27th Havas Telegram)

Capital of Yugoslavia After attending the Little Entente countries meeting, King Alexander of Yugoslavia will go to the Balchik Palace on the Black Sea coast to visit the Queen Mother of Romania (i.e., Alexander's mother-in-law) and stay there for a while. Then he will go to the port of Varna in Bulgaria to discuss the issue of mutual approach between the two countries with King Boris of Bulgaria. This cause began to be discussed in the Yugoslav capital and the Romanian Sinaia Little Entente countries meeting. This trip by the Yugoslav country is just a continuation of the previous discussion. According to reliable sources, after meeting with the Bulgarian King, Alexander will officially visit Turkish President Kemal in Turkey. (28th Havas Telegram)

Disarmament Negotiations on the Verge of Stalemate Again 55

Talk of Postponing the Meeting of the General Committee

(Geneva) Disarmament negotiations appear to be on the verge of stalemate again, and it is rumored that there are plans to postpone the meeting of the General Committee for at least two weeks. (27th Reuters Telegram)

Sato Visits Davis 56

Opposes International Management of Naval Armaments

Opposes the Big Four Monopolizing the Disarmament Issue

(Geneva) Japanese Ambassador Sato, the representative to the Disarmament Conference, met with US representative Davis on the 27th. Mr. Sato said that the United States' conditional acceptance of the international management of armaments is questionable in terms of how the international management will be applied to naval armaments. Therefore, Japan opposes the implementation of such questionable international management. He also said that the fact that France, Italy, and the United Kingdom, which left the Disarmament Conference, are discussing the disarmament issue in Rome based on the Four-Power Treaty is worrying. Representative Davis seemed to say that the United States also opposes the Disarmament Conference of only four countries. (28th Dentsu Telegram)

The League of Nations' Finances are Tight and its Activities are Reduced 57

Next Year Will Be a Year of Dormancy

Avenol Urges Countries to Pay Fees

(Geneva) The League of Nations Budget Committee met, and Secretary-General Avenol explained the financial situation. First, he reviewed the income and expenditure figures for the past years, and then discussed the budget for 1934, saying that no matter how frugal, the income will eventually be insufficient, and the scope of the League of Nations' activities will have to be reduced. He said, "We can consider next year as a year of silence, anticipation, and dormancy in some areas of activity." In reality, the serious situation may even be worse than this, and we have to completely revise what the League of Nations Assembly has decided in the past few years in order to reduce the League of Nations' theoretical activities and make them compatible with its financial capabilities. Avenol then spoke about the serious problem of some countries' arrears of dues, saying that "the League of Nations is prepared to gradually and continuously work to save expenses, but member states should also make the same efforts to pay their dues," and so on. (28th Havas Telegram)

Announcing the Reorganization of the Secretariat 58

(Geneva) The Chairman of the Supervisory Department claimed that the League of Nations Secretariat is like an army consisting entirely of generals without ordinary soldiers, with the ratio of high-paid people to low-paid people being ten to one. He also said that rationalization is the most important economic measure, especially for the Information Division, which will be completely reorganized. (27th Reuters Telegram)

Austria Leans Towards Fascism and the Socialist Party Resists 59

The Internal Guard Joins the Patriotic Front

The Strength of the Current Government is Increasing

Vienna Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss's actions to disband the Internal Guard and gradually eliminate political parties have aroused strong reactions from the Socialist Party today, declaring that if Dollfuss wants to complete his plan, it will cause a general strike or even lead to internal strife. Socialists are not as easy to deal with as Germans. At the same time, the party has convened a meeting of various trade unions and party leaders to decide on the party's future actions. However, the government's communique stated that the Internal Guard was automatically disbanded by its leaders and joined the Patriotic Front organized by Prime Minister Dollfuss. The leader of the Internal Guard also stated that this new movement has made political parties no longer necessary in the future. The statements of the party leaders and government officials all indicate that the various political parties will soon be dissolved. Socialists also believe that this movement is nothing more than a sign that Dollfuss will soon publish a fascist constitution and transform government agencies, so that it will be no different from the current German government. Furthermore, it will definitely ban trade unions. Socialists have already stated that they would not be surprised if an order to dissolve the Socialist Party is issued within 24 hours. (27th National Telegram)

Foreign Minister Hirota Calls for a Policy of Cooperation with the United States 60

The Policy Will Be Determined After Listening to Ishii's Report

The US-Japan Arbitration Treaty is Considered Possible to Realize

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Hirota will wait for the return of Plenipotentiary Ishii in October to listen to the details of the London Economic Conference. At the same time, regarding the US-Japan arbitration treaty that Plenipotentiary Ishii talked about with US President Roosevelt, he will exchange opinions frankly and without hesitation to establish future strategies and decide on policies towards the United States. Before deciding on the Empire's attitude towards the next Disarmament Conference, the new Foreign Minister will consider how to ensure the peace guarantee between Japan and the United States. He also mentioned this matter when he met with Marshals Araki and Osumi. If the current naval building competition between the United Kingdom, the United States, and Japan is left unchecked, the 1935 Disarmament Conference will inevitably fail. Therefore, it is necessary to have some kind of security guarantee coordination at this time. If this coordination is like the Manchurian issue and the Monroe Doctrine, with subtle issues of particularity, the US Senate may not object to the old situation before the treaty. From this point of view, the meeting between Foreign Minister Hirota and Plenipotentiary Ishii is extremely important. (28th Dentsu Telegram)

Pitiful Europe 61

Lloyd George Bitterly Discusses the World Situation

(Paris) The "Chronicle Magazine" will publish tomorrow an article by former British Prime Minister and Liberal Party leader Lloyd George, entitled "Wounded Europe." It begins with a semi-humorous tone, describing the current difficulties of Europe, saying that the British Empire is in better shape, and our desire to sweep the snow from our own doorstep is therefore increased. He then bitterly criticized the League of Nations, saying that it has failed in all aspects, which is a painful fact. When it comes to the German military issue, he said, "Germany is painstakingly preparing for war. We have new evidence every day of the increasing militaristic thinking of German youth. It may take Germany several years to prepare for a war, but expanding armaments is tantamount to war." He then said that most of the British public's goodwill towards Germany has recently declined significantly, due to Germany's mistreatment of Jews. After recounting Germany's isolated situation, Lloyd George said that Britain is currently very concerned about overseas colonial issues, especially the Indian issue. Finally, he mentioned Japan's naval policy, saying that Japan still wants to increase its naval power, especially its naval air power, which makes other powers with important interests in the Pacific more uneasy. This is why Britain and the United States want to maintain mutual understanding. The article ends by analyzing the U.S. economic recovery plan and praising President Roosevelt's efforts. (Havas, 28th)

Eliminating the Ills of Directive Diplomacy 62

Allowing Envoys to Freely Exercise Their Skills

(Tokyo) Since taking office, Foreign Minister Hirota has decisively reformed internal working methods. Except for important confidential telegrams, overseas telegrams do not need to be personally reviewed by the Foreign Minister. This time, the freedom of action of ambassadors stationed abroad has been expanded, allowing them to exercise their political skills and handle diplomatic affairs at their own discretion. It is said that he has also authorized representative Sawada to take appropriate measures regarding the Simla Conference, eliminating the ills of directive diplomacy. (China United News Agency, 28th)

Japanese Suspected of Secretly Photographing Fortresses 64

British Fleet Commander Denies Allegations

(Tokyo) When the British Far East Fleet submarine tender HMS Medway passed through the Shimonoseki-Moji Strait, it was discovered by officers of the Moji Maritime Police Station that they were photographing the fortress area. Russian Troops Concentrated in the Far East, a Major Threat to Japan 66

Japanese Army Ministry Denies Plans to Increase by Four Divisions

But Reforming Armaments for War Against Russia is True

(Tokyo) Reliable sources say that the concentration of Soviet Russian troops in the Far East is actually beyond expectations. It far exceeds the Second Russo-Japanese War plan attempted during the Russian imperial era. In particular, the preparation of a large number of submarines and heavy bombers that can still return after bombing the entire empire, in an attempt to disrupt the connection between the empire and the mainland, poses a major threat to Japan's national defense. Military authorities are paying close attention to the Soviet Union's active military plans. (Dentsu, 28th)

(Tokyo) The Japanese Army Ministry issued an informal statement today denying the addition of four divisions to the Japanese Army, saying that this news is untrue. The statement said in part: Recently, rumors have spread in the world that the Japanese Army Ministry has decided to increase its force by four divisions. In fact, the Army does not have a plan to increase the number of divisions, but only to improve equipment. Originally, the strength of the Japanese Army shifted in accordance with the situation on the mainland and determined its strength. After the Russo-Japanese War, in order to guard against Russian revenge, the standing army was expanded to 25 divisions. Subsequently, due to the urgent need to expand the navy domestically and the financial difficulties after the Great Kanto Earthquake, the army's funding was not secured. On the foreign front, during the European War, all Russian troops stationed in the Far East were transferred back to the Eastern Front to defend against Germany. Later, Russia underwent a revolution and was unable to take care of the Far East. Given these internal and external situations, the army adopted a policy of reducing its forces and changed the standing army to 17 divisions. Recently, the situation in Russia has changed drastically, and its military has made great progress in 15 years. Its first five-year plan has also been successful, and its domestic heavy industry and military industry have also developed greatly. Recently, its army has 75 infantry divisions and 13 cavalry divisions, totaling 990,000 men. The air force has 2,200 aircraft and 1,500 tanks. There are many new types of tanks. Since the Manchurian Incident, relations between Russia and Japan have changed, and Russia's military preparations in the Far East have also been greatly strengthened. It is said that there are ten army corps, 300 tanks, and 360 aircraft in the Far East, including dozens of the latest bombers stationed in Vladivostok, which can travel between Tokyo and Vladivostok and destroy major cities in our country. Under these circumstances, the army must be fully prepared for national defense. Recently, nationalism has spread throughout the world, and the army's equipment has also been greatly strengthened, with more emphasis on air force tanks, tank trucks, and increased firepower, so great importance is attached to machine guns. Therefore, in order to maintain the security of "Manchukuo" and be responsible for jointly defending the border, the Japanese army intends to increase various armaments, seek the mechanization of the army, and prepare sufficient firepower. This plan is a fact. As for the addition of four divisions, it is definitely a rumor. The army does not have such a plan. (China United News Agency, 28th)

New U.S. Monetary Policy 72

Aims to Fix the Price of Gold

Preventing Direct Inflation of Currency

(Washington) Key figures in U.S. financial circles claim that the U.S. President has actually drafted a new monetary policy. His trip to his Hyde Park private residence is only to make final adjustments so that he can announce it in detail. The purpose of this policy is to give gold a definite future and eliminate its uncertainty, while stimulating industry and commerce to have a more commercial level. As for its content, currency experts have not yet heard anything, but it is expected that it will not immediately inflate the currency. Officials in the Treasury Department are currently unwilling to comment on it, but according to one expert, he believes that the U.S. President's new policy will produce a gold-backed currency or commodity whose price will fluctuate with the commodity and whose gold and other metal components will be adjusted from time to time so that it can always purchase a certain amount of commodities and exchange a certain amount of services. The government's large-scale investigation of price indices has been underway for several weeks and is still continuing, but it is sufficiently complete to enable the government to obtain all the necessary information to serve as the basis for determining the price of gold. According to reliable sources, the government's adoption of this policy can greatly facilitate the negotiation of war debts because it can enable debtor countries to know the approximate value of gold in the long term to come. It is also heard that the U.S. government's adoption of this new policy is due to the enormous pressure from both the inflation and anti-inflation factions, seeking a way out and hoping to eliminate the inflation movement. According to White House sources, the U.S. President will stay at Hyde Park for a week, cutting off all political affairs and focusing on discussing currency and the recovery plan. (National News Agency, 27th)

Japanese Troops in Northeast Strictly Investigate Household Registration in All Provinces 105

Transfer Gun Ownership; Implicate the Innocent

Raise Ferocious Dogs to Specifically Harm Chinese

The Righteous Army is Active, Urgently Hoping for Supplies

Beiping Correspondence: After Ma Su entered Russia, the Righteous Army in the Northeast provinces gradually disintegrated due to the exhaustion of ammunition and supplies. Recently, in order to prevent the resurgence of the Righteous Army, the Japanese conducted a household registration survey and collected firearms. Each household must have assets of more than 5,000 yuan to be allowed to keep one gun, and a specific person must be designated to use it. If it is discovered that another person is borrowing the gun, they will be sentenced to death. In a certain village in Baiquan County, Heilongjiang Province, someone carelessly lent his family's gun to another family member. The Japanese discovered this, arrested them, and imprisoned them. The villagers, believing that they were definitely good people, jointly went to the county with more than 20 people to bail them out. The Japanese arrested all 20-plus people together, transported them in military vehicles to the village's local temple, and executed them all by shooting in public. The Japanese ruthlessly harm the Chinese in every way. Recently, at various stations along the South Manchuria Railway, they have raised many ferocious dogs. The method is to make straw figures, dress them in Chinese clothing, and hide meat in the chest and crotch areas, instructing the dogs to eat them, so that when the opportunity arises, they will specifically tear out the heart and kidneys.

The Japanese are invading our Northeast. In order to implement assimilation education, they have taken over school affairs in various provinces. In addition to changing textbooks to pro-Japanese teaching materials, Japanese language must be taught in all middle and higher schools. The positions of deans and instructors in all schools are filled by Japanese, whose authority is above that of the principal. The principals of various schools in Jiangyuan have mostly been replaced by pro-Japanese figures. The new principal of the Provincial First Normal School, a certain person from Jinzhou, held a large banquet for the school's colleagues upon taking office. Many Japanese were present and ordered him to hire prostitutes to accompany them. The principal said that hiring prostitutes at an educational banquet would harm his reputation and politely declined. The Japanese were furious and slapped the principal in the face. Seeing that the situation was not good, the principal pretended to agree to hire prostitutes and took the opportunity to escape.

In various parts of the Northeast, as the green gauze tents (tall crops that provide cover) are now rising, the Righteous Army is taking advantage of the opportunity to become active again, especially in the eastern Jilin and eastern Heilongjiang counties. However, there is a severe shortage of bullets. Recently, representatives have been sent to Guannei (within the Great Wall) to beg for assistance. The people and the Righteous Army, unable to bear the oppression and abuse of the Japanese, all hope that the national army will leave the pass as soon as possible. (Northeast News Agency)

Chiang himself, together with his wife Soong Meiling, Chief of Guards Lou Jingyue, and two attendant physicians, left the mountain early on the morning of the 22nd and took a plane back to the province in Jiujiang. In advance, the Campaign Headquarters received a phone call from Lushan and ordered the Gendarmerie Battalion, the City Defense Headquarters, and the Water and Land Public Security Bureau to strictly guard all roads from the Zhangwai River bank and the Shunwai Airport to the Campaign Headquarters and Chiang's residence in Dewai. At 12:20, Chiang's plane arrived from the north, circled the city once, and landed in the Zhangwai River. At that time, the Water Public Security Bureau had prepared a small boat and opened it to the side of the plane. Chiang then boarded the boat with his wife and landed ashore. Those who welcomed him ashore included the directors of the various departments of the Campaign Headquarters and Xiong Shihui and others. They then took cars to Chiang's private residence in Dewai. Xiong reported to Chiang on all official matters of the Campaign Headquarters, the latest bandit situation, provincial administrative facilities, the construction of the Nanchang Airport, the expansion projects of the Ji'an, Nancheng, and Linchuan airports, and all important policies for about an hour. After a short rest, He Chengjun arrived to pay his respects, reporting on the military affairs of the bandit suppression in the three provinces and requesting instructions. Huang Shaohong and Tao Jun and others arrived to pay their respects successively.

Wang Yizhe, commander of the Northeast Fourth Army, and Xiong Bin, director of the Peiping Military Affairs Commission, arrived in Xun (Jiujiang) by boat on the 22nd. On the 24th, they took the early train on the Nanxun Road to the province. After entering the city, they stayed at the provincial government guesthouse behind Maiyuan. They then went to the Campaign Headquarters to pay their respects to Chiang. It was heard that Wang reported on the content of the defense funds after the operations of the various departments in the Northeast, the recent situation of salary reductions and downsizing, the future implementation of garrison training, and requested instructions on the future policies of enriching the interior and consolidating the border defenses. Chiang gave some instructions. Xiong, on behalf of He Yingqin, reported on the downsizing and inspection methods of the various departments in North China, the negotiations on the junctions of the Great Wall, and the rampant situation of the bandit army in eastern Luan. (September 24)

Also, Chiang set off for the front on the afternoon of the 26th of this month, braving the rain to inspect military affairs and command everything. Those who came to the scene to see him off that day included Secretary-General Yang of the Campaign Headquarters, Director He Guoguang of the First Department, Director Yan Xunfu of the Second Department, Director Liu Xing of the Third Department, Zhu Huaibing, Director of the Fourth Department and concurrently Director of the Jiangxi Civil Affairs Office, and Chairman Xiong of the Provincial Government. Chiang was wearing a blue Zhongshan suit, full of energy. At 4:20, he led his secretary Deng Wenyi, Chief of Guards Lou Jingyue, and accompanying officers and soldiers to board the car and depart. It is heard that once the official business is completed, he will return to the province to control the overall military affairs.

The Fuzhou Campaign Headquarters has been formally established, and Jiang Dingwen, the commander-in-chief of the Northern Route Forward, has also taken office. (September 26)

Chairman Chiang 107

Advises Jiangxi People to Save Themselves

Those Evading Bandits Should Return to Their Villages with the Army

Strive for Self-Salvation to Achieve Survival

Nanchang Correspondence: Chairman Chiang, in view of the fact that the various armies have launched a large-scale campaign to suppress the bandits, has specially advised the virtuous gentry and people of various counties to return to their villages to save themselves and others. At the same time, he has issued an order to the various armies at the front to earnestly protect and fully cooperate with the virtuous gentry and people returning to their villages, in order to achieve twice the result with half the effort. Here is the text of his advice to the gentry and people of various counties: "The scourge of the Red Bandits in Jiangxi has been long-lasting, inhuman, and morally depraved. The people of Jiangxi have suffered from their devastation, and the number of those who have died wailing in agony is probably unknown in the millions. Their monstrous crimes have long been seen and known by the world. If they are not quickly wiped out, not only will the people of Jiangxi have no survivors, but the poison will inevitably lead to the destruction of the country and the nation.

Zhongzheng (Chiang Kai-shek referring to himself) bears the heavy responsibility of the party and the nation above, and deeply feels the suffering of the compatriots below. It is my unshirkable duty to eliminate the violence and protect the good. However, after years of deploying troops and transporting provisions, and bitter fighting, the local gentry and people have not come out to help. Society has lost its center of gravity, and the people have no leadership. The Red Bandits have taken the opportunity to seduce and coerce them. Pure and good people have followed the bandits in droves, causing the bandit flames to spread day by day, becoming a prairie fire. Thinking of this, I am deeply saddened.

You are the hope and the heart of the people of your villages. According to the principle that everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the country, how can you drift away and disregard the safety of your villages? Although it is said that the bandits hate upright people and often harm them, and that in order to protect yourselves, you have to leave your villages to avoid the danger, you should know that the Red Bandits harbor evil intentions and are by no means ordinary bandits. If you allow them to spread in the mountains and forests without eliminating them, the tragedy of destroying the countryside today will be the blueprint for trampling on the cities in the future. The only difference is the timing.

You are avoiding the cities because the countryside is dangerous, hoping to survive. If the cities are disturbed by bandits, where will you go? Where I can go, the bandits can also go. The disaster of the Red Bandits cannot be avoided by fleeing. Moreover, the cities depend on the countryside for all their food and clothing. If the countryside is in chaos for a long time, even if the cities are spared, they will eventually die of starvation. Without restoring order in the countryside to protect the source of food and clothing, and simply living in the cities, stealing a day's peace, like swallows in a hall, how long can it last? In short, we are in a position where we cannot coexist with the bandits. Either I kill the bandits, or the bandits kill me. If I do not kill the bandits, there is no way to escape death. If you do not have the determination to kill the bandits, but hide in the unproductive cities, it is like a bird avoiding the net and entering the cage, or a beast avoiding the hunt and entering the trap. There is no such thing as a cowardly and complacent person who can escape by breaking their own environment. If you do not want to save yourselves, then so be it. But if you do want to, there is no other way than to rise up and fight, cooperate with the army, and work together to eliminate the bandits.

Today, the Central Government has prepared sufficient military force and is determined to launch an attack on all fronts, with the aim of completely eliminating the bandits. This is the last day for the Red Bandits to surrender, and it is also a good opportunity for self-salvation. I hope you will not hesitate any longer, but advance with the army. Once a county is recovered, return to your villages immediately. The army will suppress them from the front, and you will clear them from the rear. You must organize the people, build blockhouses, relieve the victims, comfort the refugees, search for hidden bandits, punish the remnants, and restore the countryside. All matters relating to clearing the countryside and post-war reconstruction that the bandit suppression army cannot take care of must be carried out by you with concerted efforts. Make the people aware, so that the remnant bandits have nowhere to hide. In this way, one village will be cleared, and one county will be stabilized. We must eradicate the roots and stabilize the villages, so that there is no possibility of secret growth and we avoid repeating the mistakes of resurgence. The Red Bandits may be cunning, but they are not to be feared.

You save others by saving yourselves, and you save the country by saving your villages. In the future, when the bandit suppression is successful, Zhongzheng will investigate your actions, record your achievements, report them to the Central Government, and give you generous rewards. If there are those who are brave enough to go to justice, who are injured in the line of duty, or who die in the line of duty, they will be given generous compensation to show our shared hardship. I have already ordered the military and political officers at the front to treat the returning natives with love and cooperate with sincerity, in order to help and support each other. In the past, Zeng Guofan rose from the local militia and quelled the Taiping Rebellion. The reason for his success was that he relied on the voluntary assistance of the people. The lessons of the past are not far away and can be learned from. I believe that you will respect your homeland and be eager to save yourselves, so you will surely rise up and compete, and do not need Zhongzheng's earnest advice. Go forth and work hard, and may you all strive to do your best. (September 23)

Anhui Province Rice Industry Improvement Conference 109

Construction Bureau Sends Staff to Wuhu

General Assembly Convened in the Chamber of Commerce

Wuhu Correspondence: The Anhui Construction Bureau, in order to discuss the methods of relieving rural undertakings, investigate the past production and sales of rice in Wuhu, the current fact that the rice market is stagnant, and the trade situation of rice merchants in various places, in order to formulate methods to adjust smooth sales, and establish a system of warehouses to store grain for famine relief, has specially sent Commissioner Chen Bikuan to Wuhu to work with the Administrative Commissioner's Office and the Wuhu Chamber of Commerce to plan comprehensively. After Chen arrived in Wuhu, he conducted investigations in various aspects and convened a general meeting at the County Chamber of Commerce at 2:00 PM this (23rd) afternoon. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Proposal to revitalize the local rice industry. Resolution: Domestic rice is stagnant in sales. It should be requested that the government increase the import tax rate on foreign rice by 30%. Commissioner Chen Bikuan will, based on the resolution, submit it to the Provincial and Municipal Governments for submission to the Headquarters and the government agencies for approval. (2) Proposal to prohibit the mixing of water and sand in rice and grain. Resolution: The Commissioner's Office should earnestly investigate and prohibit it and announce the prohibition. If there are any violations, severe punishments will be imposed. (3) How to reduce the expenses of Wuhu rice merchants. Resolution: The County Government should convene the Chamber of Commerce and relevant groups, such as the transportation industry, Guangchao Yanning rice industry, mill industry, rice industry, rice milling industry, and miscellaneous grain industry, within this month to jointly discuss and resolve it. (4) Changing the rice industry from liang to yuan should be included in the above meeting and the date of implementation should be determined. (5) How to eliminate the bad habit of hooligans demanding money. Resolution: The rice and grain industry should submit the actual situation of various demands to the County Government and devise ways to strictly prohibit it. (23rd)

Songjiang

Wu Sheng Robbed in Zhujiahang 110

Wu Youlan, a resident of Zhubin Hang Town, Tinglin County, is a wealthy gentleman in the town, leading him to be coveted by bandits. On the evening of the 25th, taking advantage of the rainy weather, more than a dozen bandits speaking the local dialect dug through the back wall of his house, sneaked in, removed the latch from the back door, and rushed in. They went upstairs together, tied up the victim Wu Lu and coerced him to give them money, but failed. They burned his chest. His nephew Youzhu stepped forward to intercede and was shot by the bandits. They then went into various rooms to rob more than 1,000 yuan in cash and more than 20 pieces of gold jewelry. The robbery lasted for about three hours. It was not until 1:00 AM that they left with the loot. The town's land and water police group heard the news and pursued them, but they had disappeared. The second branch of Tinglin and the security group also reported by telephone and rushed to investigate that night. Wu Lu, who is over sixty years old, was seriously injured and has been treated by himself. He has also reported to the court to request a search and arrest.

Son Injures Father-in-Law who Committed Adultery with his Wife 111

Zhou Jingui, a Jiangbei migrant with the nickname "Duck [Obscenity]", is nearly fifty years old. His wife, Zhu, has two sons. The eldest son, A Da, has a child bride He, who was married last year. After the marriage, her father-in-law did not allow his son to live with her. The father-in-law and daughter-in-law rented a house and lived separately. Today (the 28th) morning, Jin Gui and his wife had an argument, which led to a fight. The two sons helped their mother and beat their father, Jin Gui, injuring his head, hands, and legs, causing him to bleed profusely. Jin Gui reported to the first branch office to arrest the murderous sons for investigation. It is rumored that Jin Gui committed adultery with his daughter-in-law, and his son had harbored resentment for a long time, which led to today's incident. It is heard that the case will be transferred to the court for investigation.

Suzhou

White Dragon Port Pig Boat Robbed 112

In the Bailonggang area of Wujiang County, a pig boat belonging to Liu Zirang was passing through the area on the afternoon of the 27th when it was suddenly encountered by a bandit boat coming from the north. It carried nine male and female bandits armed with box cannons. They rushed to the boat and arbitrarily searched for clothes and silver dollars, totaling more than 200 yuan, and left. The incident was learned by the fifteenth team of the Third District of the Water Public Security Bureau. Captain Wu led the police to pursue them, but they had already escaped.

Judgment on Trafficking of People 113

The "Queen of the Flesh Forest" Li Sanyuan's case of trafficking in persons, after the Public Security Bureau arrested the young girls Zhu Xiudi and others, and also arrested Li's father Guiqing, and the procuress Wang Ni, was transferred to the local court. Yesterday (the 28th), the verdict was announced: Wu Guiqing was sentenced to six months imprisonment, Wang Ni and Tang Pu were each sentenced to three months imprisonment, and Shi Chen was sentenced to two months imprisonment, with a two-year reprieve. Zhu Xiudi and others were taken back by their families.

Wuxi

Long-Distance Bus Overturns and Causes Disaster 114

The Xicheng Long-Distance Bus Company has repeatedly caused major disasters since it was established. At 7:30 AM yesterday (the 28th), the company's No. 2 bus, loaded with more than 20 passengers from Cheng (Jiangyin), started to drive to Xi (Wuxi). At 8:20, when the bus was driving through Bantang Temple in the Sixth District of Xijing, the "Axle Xiaozi" (transliteration) on the wheel suddenly broke, and the bus went straight into the river on the left. The driver, Wang Leshan (28 years old, from Hangzhou), was caught off guard, causing the entire bus to fall into the river. The passengers in the bus were panic-stricken, and the sound of shouting for help and crying shook the fields. Fortunately, the driver Wang Leshan came up with a clever idea and immediately opened the glass windows on the car. He climbed ashore and saw that there were vegetable farmers on the shore. He immediately called the farmers to smash all the glass windows with carrying poles and other things. Then, the passengers in the car were pulled out one by one. However, one female passenger (about 40 years old, name unknown) was too seriously injured and died. Among the others who were seriously injured, there were ten people, including Yang Pinglv and Yu Shengrong. Nine people, including Xu Ji'an and Ren You, were slightly injured. The driver telegraphed to the Wuxi Long-Distance Bus Company, which rushed to send a small car to the scene to take the ten seriously injured to the Tongren Hospital for treatment. The nine slightly injured were taken to the Fensi Center and doctors were called to treat them. At the same time, County Magistrate Yan Shenyu also received the news and went to inspect the scene in person. The first police station of the twelfth branch of the Public Security Bureau also sent police to the scene to suppress the situation. As for the corpse, it was still placed on the bank there. At 3:00 PM, the head of the second and eighth districts, Shen Debiao, reported to the County Court, and the prosecutor led the staff to the scene to verify the injury and death. Because no family members were found, they took photos and ordered the head of the district to arrange for coffins and burial on their behalf, and wait for the family members to claim them after investigation.

Discharged Soldier Commits Suicide Due to Heartbreak 115

Sun Yecheng, 32 years old, from Pukou, was formerly a policeman in the fifth and first branches of the local Public Security Bureau. Later, he was dismissed due to an incident and changed to be a messenger in the Fifth Regiment of the Garrison in Wuxi. When the Garrison was transferred to Han Gao, Sun also went west with the army. However, when he was in Wuxi, he had an affair with Wang Aimei's daughter Yuying, who sells sugar-roasted sweet potatoes in the Huangting Temple in Chong'an Temple. Yuying is now 18 years old and has a fiery relationship with Sun. After Sun went to Han, he missed her because of the separation of the two lovers. Looking back on the past, he suddenly had the idea of giving up the world. On the 13th of this month, he committed suicide by taking poison in Han. Soldiers in the same camp discovered it and reported it to their superiors. He was treated and recovered. From then on, Sun was dismissed again by his superiors. On the 18th, he came to Wuxi after traveling from Han. In the afternoon, he stayed in Room 43 of the Da Zhonghua Hotel on the Railway Station Road. That night, he secretly took one yuan of raw opium and committed suicide. Yesterday, the tea servant Shen A Da discovered it and immediately sent him to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. Two letters were also found in his room, one to his lover Wang Yuying, the content was full of tender love and he couldn't bear to finish reading it, and one to the hotel manager, asking him to ask the court to waive the inspection. It is now heard that after entering the hospital, his life may be saved.

Changzhou

Guanyintang Village Robbery and Assault 116

Last night (the 27th) around midnight, a group of twelve armed bandits broke into the home of Wang Yida, a villager in Guanyintang Village near Gangqiao in the 14th District of Wuyi, and began looting. Wang Yida and his tenant farmer, Chen Quangen, hid upstairs but were spotted by the bandits, who immediately dragged them down and demanded to know where the silver was hidden. Gunshots were heard, and both were injured and fell to the ground. The bandits searched for about an hour before fleeing with a whoop. The injured Wang Yida and Chen Quangen were transported to Wuyi Hospital for treatment today (the 28th). However, the bullets remain lodged in their bodies and require surgery. Fortunately, the injuries are not to vital organs, and their lives are not in danger.

Rugao

Hurricane Capsizes Pig Boat 118

In Shijiazhuang, Chema Lake District, Rugao, a man named Xue He, who makes a living by sailing, bought a large boat last year for 1,000 yuan, capable of carrying several hundred people. He recently repainted it, making it look brand new. Several days ago, he partnered with others to buy over eighty healthy pigs to sell in Jiangnan. While sailing to Fukou Port, they suddenly encountered a hurricane, with white waves surging several yards high. The boat could not anchor and was capsized into the river by a huge wave and swept away. Fortunately, Xue was rescued by a neighboring boat and survived. However, all eighty-odd healthy pigs drowned, and a boatman named Li is also missing. The losses are estimated to be over 5,000 yuan.

Kidnapping Occurs in Gaozi Township 119

In Zhangjiagang, Gaizi South, in the western part of the county, a villager named Wang Shanjun, over thirty years old and a bricklayer by trade, was kidnapped. Because of his diligence and thrift, his family enjoyed a modest prosperity. However, his wealth attracted the attention of bandits. The other night after 9:00 PM, a dozen or so bandits suddenly rushed into his house and abducted Wang. Yesterday morning, Wang's wife found a letter in the doorway stating that 3,000 silver dollars were required for ransom. She should wait for three days and then go to Wuli Mountain outside the South Gate, using a towel hanging from a bamboo pole as a signal. Wang's wife received the letter and is extremely anxious because raising the ransom money will be difficult.

Yixing

Promoting Stamp Sales Triggers Market Strike 120

On September 16th, at around 4:00 PM, Lu Zhongwu and two other employees from the Yixing Stamp Tax Bureau went to Hengtaihe Shoe and Hat Store on East Main Street to promote the sale of five yuan in stamps. The shop assistant refused, saying that the owner was out and the store already had a large stock of stamps, so they could not accept them without authorization. Lu and the others then entered the accounting area and took two or three ledgers, claiming that some stamps were not affixed, and that they should be punished according to the regulations. At this point, the shop assistant shouted that they had broken into the accounting area and lost 300 silver dollars. The owner, Jiang Qianxing, rushed back upon hearing the news and argued with them. The bureau employees reported the incident to the Jiaoxiao Gang police and requested assistance from the Public Security Bureau. As a result, all the large and small shops on East Main Street considered this a disturbance to their business and declared a strike. The Public Security Bureau, upon learning of the news, feared that the situation would escalate and took Lu Zhongwu into custody to appease the public. The Chamber of Commerce chairman, Yu Xunlu, urged them to reopen the market along the way and, at around 6:00 PM that afternoon, convened an emergency meeting of representatives from various shops on East Main Street to discuss solutions.

Local News

Eurasia Aviation Corporation Manager Li Jingcong Returns from the Northwest Yesterday 122

No Need for Lanzhou-Qinghai Line Trial Flight Yet

Luo Wengan Already in Tacheng Meeting with Yan Envoy

Eurasia Through Transport Can Be Implemented Soon

Li Jingcong, manager of the Eurasia Aviation Corporation, returned to Shanghai yesterday morning after departing from Shanghai last Wednesday to inspect the company's situation along the line in the Northwest and conduct a test flight on the Qinghai line. A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency visited Mr. Li in the afternoon and discussed the following items.

Satisfied with On-Site Inspection 123

According to Mr. Li's statement to the Xinsheng News Agency, his trip to the Northwest had three objectives: (1) to inspect the construction and operation of the company's stations along the line; (2) to thank the local authorities for their assistance; (3) to conduct a test flight on the branch line from Lanzhou to Qinghai. The situation was excellent from Shanghai to Hami. However, due to unrest in the area from Hami to Dihua and the limited time, he quickly returned and will inspect it again next time.

Suspension of Qinghai Branch Line Development 124

After arriving in Lanzhou on the return trip, he immediately conducted a test flight on the Qinghai branch line. As a result, he felt that although the distance between Qinghai and Lanzhou was 200 kilometers, transportation was very convenient. It could be reached by car in only one day, or at most one and a half days, so mail delivery would only take thirty-six hours. Also, since there were almost no passengers and airfare was too expensive, it was not very suitable for the people of that area. Therefore, there was no need to open a route for the time being. The Qinghai Provincial Government's airfield is well-equipped and can be used at any time if necessary, either once a week or once every two weeks.

Through Transport Awaits Gasoline. He also said that the plans for the Beiping-Suiyuan and Shanghai-Guangdong lines had been prepared long ago. However, both lines are completely related to the Eurasia through transport, so they must wait until the Eurasia through transport can be realized before they can be opened at the same time. As for the Eurasia through transport, the only problem now is gasoline. After ordering Russian oil, it has been reported that it has already begun to be transported to Tacheng. However, the company has not yet received a formal report. Once this gasoline problem is officially telegraphed as resolved and delivered, the through transport will be officially opened and implemented.

Luo Awaits Yan at Russian Border. Furthermore, he stated that the market in the Hami area was very depressed after the war and that the local area was currently peaceful. Chairman Ma of Qinghai recently went to Lanzhou to meet with Chairman Zhu Shaoliang of Gansu to discuss everything. It is expected that he has already returned to Qinghai within a few days. Reports that Ma Zhongying's troops attacked Xinjiang Province and intercepted the gasoline for the company's plane carrying Minister Luo to Xinjiang are not accurate. Our company is commercial in nature and has good relations with the local garrisons. The Lanzhou-Hami route is still operating as usual. Because he did not inquire about the conflict between Sheng and Ma, he did not want to talk about it further. However, he heard that Minister Luo had gone to Tacheng and transferred to Novosbirsk on the Russian border to meet with Ambassador Yan.

China National Aviation Corporation Suspends Shanghai-Guangdong Route 125

The China National Aviation Corporation's plan to establish the Shanghai-Guangdong air trunk line has been delayed to this day due to various political factors. After a successful trial flight last month, it was planned to start operations. The Guangdong side showed some dissatisfaction with the flight of this line. Recently, they established the Southwest Aviation Corporation. In order to avoid conflicts in routes and business, China National Aviation Corporation decided to suspend the Shanghai-Guangdong route. However, the Sino-American joint flight plan will continue to be implemented.

Report on Disaster Situation. After performing the rituals, (1) Bao Tigan, the acting magistrate of Baoshan County, reported on the disaster in the five sands of Baoshan County, stating that Changxing Sand, Dongxin Sand, Ping'an Sand, Ruifeng Sand, and Shitou Sand were affected by the tidal surge, resulting in the drowning of forty-four men, women, and children, the destruction of 1,799 houses, and damage to 517 houses. Repairs to official works and embankment are estimated to require 112,000 yuan. (2) Shen Jiang, the magistrate of Chongming County, reported that the county was severely affected by a sudden hurricane, coupled with the surge of floods. All districts and Shengsi Island were severely affected, with the disaster area spanning 57 townships, covering an area of more than 700 square li. More than 203,000 mu of farmland were affected, and more than 6,380 houses were lost. The number of victims and deaths totaled more than 21,500. Grain and houses were completely swept away. Looking at the disaster area, it was a heartbreaking sight. In addition, the coastal seawall, which was more than sixty li long, was almost completely destroyed this time. The project is huge and requires more funding. (3) Fei Gongxia, the magistrate of Qidong County, reported that the disaster area accounted for about 30% of the county's total area, with the seventh and eighth districts along the coast being the most severely affected. The main crop in the county is cotton. This year, the seventh and eighth districts mostly planted improved cotton, which was expected to yield a bumper harvest. However, after two floods, the cotton harvest was hopeless, and the food harvested by the farmers was also swept away by the tide. Since the dike body was broken, the low-lying areas are still mostly submerged in water during high tide. Therefore, in addition to providing emergency relief for the food, clothing, and shelter of the victims, it is also necessary to quickly repair the collapsed dikes.

Resolutions. After the reports, discussions began. (1) The chairman proposed that the association be merged with the Pudong Chuannan Typhoon Relief Association and renamed the "Jiangsu Coastal Counties Flood Relief Association" in order to pool efforts and work together for mutual benefit. (Resolution) The association will appoint three representatives to contact the Pudong and Chuannan Relief Association to discuss the merger methods. (2) For emergency relief, the minimum emergency relief fund for the clothing, food, and shelter of the victims in the five counties is estimated to be 300,000 yuan, and the repair of the collapsed dikes is not included. Please decide how to resolve this. (Resolution) While proceeding with the merger, fundraising should begin immediately to provide emergency relief. In addition, three representatives will be appointed to go to the province to request the government to repair the dikes of the five counties. (3) Appointment of representatives to contact the Pudong Chuannan Relief Association and representatives to go to the province. (Resolution) It was decided to appoint Wang Dankui, representative of Chongming County, Gu Nanqun, representative of Qidong County, and Jin Houcheng, representative of Baoshan County, to be responsible for the proceedings. (4) The detailed procedures of the association will be discussed at the next joint meeting. (Resolution) Passed. The meeting adjourned after other minor matters.

Post-Typhoon Relief Efforts in Shanghai 129

The Municipal Authorities Are Proceeding

Due to the typhoon that struck the city this time, all farmers along the coast and rivers have been displaced due to the destruction of their homes and fields. The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has convened a meeting with the Land and Public Works Bureaus to discuss relief measures. According to Wu Huanru, the chief of the Second Section of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, the relief situation is as follows:

Emergency Construction of Dikes. On the dike construction front, the Eastern Dike has more damage than the Western Dike, which has no major destruction. The municipal government has allocated 50,000 yuan to the Municipal Public Works Bureau to actively repair it. The bureau has dispatched a large number of workers, supervised by Dai Erjing, the director of the Dike Construction Section, to carry out the repairs. The situation is now under control.

Repair of Embankments. The embankments along Huangpu River on Jungong Road have been severely damaged. There are currently more than 1,000 mu of embanked fields in that area, which are leased to farmers by the Zuohai Company, operated by Zhang Xiaoruo, Rong Zongjing, and Jin Qushan. However, the embanked fields in that area have never had a bumper year due to the rising river water. This year, they were almost completely washed away, resulting in the waste of the farmers' hard work throughout the year. The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has convened the Municipal Affairs Committee member Zhu Jiajun and the Zuohai Company shareholder Zhang Xiaoruo to discuss relief measures. The company stated that the embanked fields have been losing money every year since the company started operating them, so it is impossible to allocate funds for relief. After repeated discussions, the company agreed that the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, the Municipal Affairs Committee Office, and the company will jointly raise a considerable amount of money to hire the farmers in that area to repair the embankments, which will achieve two goals at once.

Relief for Villagers. The losses suffered by the farmers in Gaoqiao and other districts are relatively large. The Social Affairs Bureau and others have sent personnel to investigate and comfort the villagers, and local charitable organizations have gone to provide relief, distributing 20 cents of food per person per day, with half for children. Fortunately, the number of people is small, and there are no major difficulties in raising funds. As for the request to waive the field tax in the district, it should be given due consideration. However, there are many twists and turns in the procedures for waiving the tax, and it may be difficult to make a decision within the year. However, if the government believes that it is indeed necessary to reduce or waive the field tax, it can find a way to offset it next year.

First Batch of American Cotton to Arrive Today or Tomorrow 130

Office Held Meeting Yesterday to Discuss Sales Methods

Hired Zhang Gongquan and Three Others as Promotion Commissioners

Rong Zongjing Discusses that Chinese Factories Decide to Purchase as Much as Possible

The first batch of American cotton purchased by China from the US loan is on the Fook Lai & Co. "Essian Allen" (transliterated) and is expected to arrive in Shanghai today or tomorrow. The Ministry of Finance will hire Zhang Gongquan and others as promotion commissioners. Xi Demao, director of the US Loan Cotton and Wheat Office of the Central Bank, held a meeting with sales firms and others yesterday to discuss methods. Cotton magnate Rong Zongjing made a statement. Details are as follows:

First Batch of American Cotton to Arrive Today or Tomorrow. Xinsheng News Agency reported that the first batch of American cotton loaded on the Fook Lai & Co. "Essian Allen" sailed to Shanghai on August 15th in America. The Shanghai Fook Lai & Co. received a radio report on the itinerary the day before yesterday and is expected to arrive in Shanghai this afternoon and will dock at the China Merchants Bureau wharf in Pudong. It will arrive no later than tomorrow morning. The manager of Fook Lai & Co. has notified the head of the boat room and will send personnel to the wharf to make arrangements. The ship's manifest has arrived in Shanghai.

Yesterday's Meeting in Strict Secrecy. Xi Demao, director of the US Loan Cotton and Wheat Office of the Central Bank, held a meeting at the Central Bank at 3:00 PM yesterday with the Western managers of cotton firms such as Fook Lai, Anli, and Mei'an, which handle the sale of cotton, to discuss the sales of American cotton after it arrives in Shanghai. It did not end until around 4:00 PM. When reporters inquired with the director of the US Loan Cotton and Wheat Office, they all kept it strictly confidential, and Fook Lai and other firms also remained silent because they feared that the news would affect market prices.

Business Magnates Promote American Cotton. A Central News Agency reporter visited Rong Zongjing yesterday morning, who stated that American cotton has been shipped to China one after another from the United States. The first batch of cotton will arrive in Shanghai within a few days. The Central Bank has established an office to take charge of all matters related to American cotton after it arrives in Shanghai. As for the promotion personnel, Minister Song has hired Zhang Gongquan, General Manager of the Bank of China, Chen Guangfu, General Manager of the Shanghai Bank, Guo Shun, General Manager of the Wing On Textile Factory, and myself. Therefore, we plan to gather and discuss promotion methods within a few days. As for the sales channel of American cotton after it arrives in Shanghai, it is an important issue. In recent years, Chinese textile factories have reduced labor due to sluggish sales and overproduction. Cotton accumulation is inevitable. In addition, the rural economy is on the verge of bankruptcy. Cash in various places is concentrated in Shanghai. Banks only accept credit and do not release loans. As a result, the financial situation in various places is far from what it used to be. The weakness of purchasing power in various ports is not only the case for American cotton. Moreover, the price of American cotton is higher than that of domestic cotton, so sales become a problem.

Chinese Merchants Stop Ordering Directly. It was previously rumored that Chinese textile factories were unwilling to buy American cotton, which is not accurate. Since Minister Song signed a US$50 million cotton and wheat loan in the United States, Chinese textile factories in this city have stopped ordering American cotton directly from the United States. Each factory knows that a whole number of American cottons have been shipped to China, so there is no need to order goods from the United States again. In the future, American textile factories will purchase American cotton from the government if they need it. The attitude of the Chinese merchants has already expressed cooperation with the government. As for Japanese merchants buying American cotton, Minister Song has also said that it is difficult for commercial organizations selling goods to distinguish which country's merchants are buying.

Sales of American Wheat Are Extremely Difficult. There is no exact date for American wheat to be shipped to Shanghai. At this time when rice prices are low in our country, the sales of expensive American wheat shipped to China is even more difficult. Moreover, wheat flour stocks are piling up in various ports. It is estimated that there are more than 4 million dans stored in Shanghai and Tianjin. It is estimated that such a large amount of stored wheat can be sold out in half a year, so the sales of American wheat need to be studied.

Anhui Province Sheyu Road Public Bond Held Lottery Repayment in Shanghai Yesterday 131

Six Tranche Drawn, Principal and Interest of 50,000 Yuan

Paid by the Agricultural and Industrial Bank at the End of This Month

The Anhui Province Sheyu Highway Public Bond held its first lottery repayment in Shanghai yesterday afternoon.

Attending Representatives. Liu Yiyan, director of the Anhui Provincial Department of Construction, Lu Wenshao, City Chamber of Commerce, Wu Bicai, Municipal Government, Ye Fuxiao, Bankers' Association, Qi Yunqing, Fund Management Committee, Cheng Zhuxin, Hangzhou China Agricultural and Industrial Bank, Mao Yun, Municipal Party Department, Xu Chuanyou, Zhang Jun, Han Jun, Liu Zhongya, Li Dafu, Solicitation Officer, Cheng Kefan, Jixi Fellow Association, Cao Zhigong, Huining Fellow Association, Xu Yunsong, She County Fellow Association, Zheng Jianzhen, Wuyuan Fellow Association, and others, totaling more than thirty people.

Chairman's Report. Chairman Cheng Zhuxin reported that Huizhou in southern Anhui is located in the midst of thousands of mountains, and transportation has always been inconvenient. Nine out of ten Huizhou people are engaged in business outside, and every time they have to travel with difficulty, they do not return for many years. The tea, Huizhou ink, compasses, sundials, bronze ware, etc. produced there are also loved at home and abroad. Export is already difficult, and the import of goods such as salt, rice, silk, cloth, groceries, etc. is even more expensive. In order to promote transportation and develop industry, the construction of highways is the most urgent task. The governments of Zhejiang and Anhui provinces have close business and travel relations and are seeking to develop transportation. Therefore, they created the Hangzhou-Huizhou Highway, including the section from She County to Yuling Pass, which is more than 70 kilometers long, with rugged mountains and difficult construction. Anhui Province has relatively difficult finances and has to raise special funds. Therefore, it issued 500,000 yuan of Sheyu Highway Public Bonds, with 98% actually received, divided into sixteen repayments over eight years, and giving 8% annual interest. Ordinary business tax revenue of 100,000 yuan per year is allocated and deposited in the China Agricultural and Industrial Bank as a repayment fund for capital and interest. The Sheyu Highway Fund Management Committee is specially established, with two people elected by the bondholders, one manager of the bank where the funds are stored, and one representative each from the Anhui Provincial Government and the two departments of finance and construction, to form a joint organization. Now it is the time for the first repayment, and it is specifically scheduled for 3:00 PM on September 28th to perform the lottery in the banking industry association in Shanghai. The Anhui Provincial Government sends a letter to various groups in Shanghai to send representatives to supervise the ceremony, and also invites the committees from Huizhou Fellow Association in Shanghai who solicited public bonds to come and visit. Then Liu Yiyan, Mao Yun, Wu Bicai, Lu Wenshao, etc. gave speeches one after another. The wording is omitted.

Winning Numbers. Then the supervisors Cao Shuqin and Li Dafu reviewed the lottery tickets to make sure they were correct. Then, lottery drawers Wu Zhiping and Zheng Jianyuan performed the lottery and drew six. At the end of this month, the Shanghai-Hangzhou local Agricultural and Industrial Bank and the county governments of Anhui Province will issue the numbers: "No. 08", "No. 23", "No. 39", "No. 54", "No. 76", "No. 89". The above six winning numbers are the last two digits of the bond number. Anyone holding this bond, whether it is a hundred-yuan ticket, a ten-yuan ticket, or a five-yuan ticket, only needs the last two digits to be the same as the winning number, and can redeem the principal and the current interest from the local China Agricultural and Industrial Banks in Shanghai and Hangzhou and the county governments in Anhui Province at the end of this month.

Factory Inspection Negotiations 132

Ministry of Industry Instructions on Policy

Regarding the Shanghai factory inspection issue, the Shanghai Municipal Council has requested supervisory and directing authority. The Shanghai Municipal Government has requested instructions from the government. The Ministry of Industry has ordered that the original policy be carried out, adhering to the principle of not losing sovereignty. The Ministry believes that factory inspection is our country's implementation of the Factory Inspection Law within its own territory. In theory, the Municipal Council should not obstruct it. Moreover, our proposal at that time had been slightly modified, with the Municipal Council also sending personnel to participate. However, still wanting to request supervisory and directing authority seems to be an excessive demand. This matter must wait until the Municipal Council Board of Directors meeting when Feixin Dun (transliteration) will report the results of the consultation, and then the Board of Directors will discuss it before a decision can be made. As for factory inspections in other places such as Wuhan, Shanghai, and Qingdao, it will be smoother to implement them after this matter is resolved. The factory inspection plan for the 22nd year is also planned to be started after the resolution. The plan has been sent to the Executive Yuan and should be passed within a few days.

Nanjing-Shanghai Long Distance Telephone 133

Ministry of Communications Decides to Add New Lines

The spokesperson of the Ministry of Communications said that there are often cases where it takes several hours to connect after registering for a Nanjing-Shanghai long-distance telephone call because the original telephone poles are full. It is not enough to meet the needs without adding new lines. Now the Ministry of Communications has ordered the Nanjing-Shanghai Highway to set up a new line, starting from Nanjing, passing through Jurong, Liyang, Yixing, Wuxi, Changshu, Taicang, Jiading, and reaching Shanghai, 232 miles long. After the line is completed, there will be six telephone return lines. It can be completed and put into service within four months.

Ministry of Communications Cracks Down on Fictitious Shipping Companies 136

The Shanghai Navigation Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, in order to crack down on fictitious shipping companies, drafted several suggestions and submitted them to the Ministry, requesting that the Ministry of Industry be consulted for verification and compliance. Yesterday, the Ministry's order was received, stating: "The submission has been noted. The three measures proposed for cracking down on fictitious shipping companies have some inappropriate aspects. The Ministry has revised them based on the circumstances as follows: (1) New shipping bureaus or companies, in addition to complying with the Company Law, should submit to the competent Navigation Administration Bureau for approval the amount of capital prepared, the number and names of ships, a statement indicating whether they are owned or leased, the resumes of the responsible personnel of the shipping bureau or company, and the main operating routes. (2) After a new shipping bureau or company has been reported and approved, all its ships should be declared for measurement or inspection, and business can only commence after certificates have been issued. (3) New shipping bureaus or companies must not engage in any external publicity or advertising before completing the above two procedures. Violators may be informed by the competent Navigation Administration Bureau to the local police station to order a cessation of activities." In addition to consulting with the Ministry of Industry for verification, the order instructs the various shipping industry associations and informs all shipping merchants to comply. The Bureau has already forwarded the order to various shipping companies and offices and sent a letter to the Shanghai Shipping Industry Association for verification.

Prince Wang's Department Cables Request for Ammunition and Supplies Due to Shortages 137

The Shanghai Liaison Office of the Third Route of the Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army recently received a cable from Wang Zezhou, commander of the Second Column of the Route, from the front lines. He reported that the Japanese military police battalion chief, Sawakawababe, and the troops led by Yu Tianmin of the puppet army under Li Shouxin had joined forces in the Yangri and Xinxingzi areas in Rehe Province and were advancing on our army at night. The First Detachment Commander, Wan Kecheng, bravely resisted, engaging in fierce fighting for two days and nights. At dawn on the last day, nine enemy bombers suddenly appeared, dropping dozens of bombs. Unfortunately, nearby villages and houses were destroyed, and over two hundred villagers were killed or injured. Those who could not escape were bombed to death. Detachment Commander Wan Kecheng used Russian-style linked machine guns to shoot down one enemy plane. The remaining planes retreated with injuries. However, due to the intense enemy artillery fire and the shortage of food and ammunition, our army found it difficult to resist. While engaged in hand-to-hand combat, the First Column under Yang Xianfu, stationed at Mojiazi, fortunately rushed to reinforce us, bravely intercepting the enemy and repelling them, thwarting their attack. However, our army is currently short of food and ammunition, so a special cable was sent to the rear requesting supplies and replenishment of military equipment to prepare for any eventuality. Five Japanese officers, thirteen puppet officers, and seventy-two soldiers were captured. In this battle, our army suffered over five hundred casualties. The seriously wounded officers and soldiers have been cared for and sent to the rear for medical treatment through the efforts of Commander-in-Chief Zhu. Those killed in action include Captain Zhai Haiyun, Battalion Adjutant Jiang Yibo, Company Commanders Shi Zhizhong, Company Adjutants Yu Dingyi and Cheng Zhiyuan, Squad Leaders Hu Sien, Qu Liben, and Zhang Dagong, Squad Adjutants Huang Dongsheng, Sheng Zuo, and Bai Deyi, and Platoon Leaders Yang Chonghan and Lü Shiwu. The enemy suffered heavy casualties, and we captured ninety-seven rifles, twelve hand-held weapons, two mortars, three heavy machine guns, two small steel cannons, one tank, and some military supplies.

Chuansha: A telegram from the Chuansha Flood Relief Association to Du Yuesheng, Wang Yiting, Wang Xiaolai, and Huang Hanzhi reads: "Du Yuesheng, Wang Yiting, Wang Xiaolai, and Huang Hanzhi, esteemed sirs, Chuansha is unfortunate to have suffered repeated natural disasters.
