The tragic situation is heartbreaking to witness. We previously received relief funds allocated by you, which have been distributed, benefiting the disaster victims. We express our deep gratitude. However, the disaster is severe, and there are many refugees. The relief funds raised may not be widespread enough. We have heard that you will provide ample relief to rescue those in danger, and we are deeply grateful. Faced with the cries of the hungry and distressed, those who are not sick urgently need food and clothing, and those who are sick need medicine. Therefore, we urgently request you to allocate food, clothing, and medicine as soon as possible for distribution to alleviate the immediate crisis, which would be extremely fortunate. Currently, disaster victims are everywhere, supporting the old and carrying the young, crying from cold and hunger, living in the open air, in a precarious state. We have heard that you uphold the righteousness of helping disaster-stricken neighbors and practice the benevolence of feeding the hungry and rescuing the drowning, sparing no effort to inspect the disaster areas. We are deeply moved and grateful. If your visit is scheduled, please inform us in advance so that we can follow you and be available for inquiries. We eagerly anticipate your arrival. Li Lenggan, Magistrate of Chuansha County and Chairman of the Relief Committee, respectfully."

Zhenhai: The Ningbo Native Place Association received a disaster report letter from Xu Yong, Magistrate of Zhenhai County, stating: "Zhenyi suffered from two typhoons and rainstorms on the evening of September 1st and 18th, with the 18th being particularly severe. The tide rose sharply, with the water along the river reaching depths of over ten feet. Houses, boats, salt fields, dikes, and dams were severely damaged. Cotton crops failed, and there is no hope for the autumn harvest of rice. The harvest is halved. Disaster-stricken households account for two-tenths of the entire county, approximately 30,000 households. Eight men and women drowned. It is estimated that over 300 brick houses were destroyed, several thousand were partially destroyed, and over 1,000 thatched houses were completely destroyed, with losses of approximately 300,000 yuan. Over 100 boats of various sizes were lost, with losses of 5,000 to 6,000 yuan. Several thousand salt slabs and 200,000 to 300,000 catties of salt were washed away, along with salt field constructions, estimated at over 100,000 yuan. The outer dikes along the coast were all destroyed, and there are many missing fields in the inner dikes. The coastal area of the entire county spans approximately 200 li. It is estimated that repairs will cost over 500,000 yuan. Over 100,000 mu of cotton fields suffered a complete crop failure, with estimated losses of over 1,200,000 yuan. The rice harvest is halved, with losses of approximately 1,000,000 yuan. The total estimated losses exceed 3,000,000 yuan. After days of investigation, I see devastation everywhere, with wails of distress echoing across the land. It is a rare disaster unseen in decades, even more severe than the autumn disaster of twenty years ago. In addition to urging local autonomous personnel to repair the dikes and dams on the spot and opening all the sluice gates at the same time to drain the saltwater from the inner rivers, I am also advising farmers to use waterwheels to irrigate their fields to wash away the saltwater. At the same time, I am sending telegrams to the provincial authorities requesting disaster relief and planning to organize work relief. However, the provincial and county treasuries are empty. The funds allocated in the future will definitely be limited. Soon it will be mid-winter, and the helpless disaster victims are in danger of freezing and starving. Among the dikes, apart from private dikes, the most important official dikes are the Houhai Dike and the Shitou Dike, with as many as sixty or seventy breaches. The funds required are enormous, and it is difficult to raise them. Fellow villagers from Zhenyi in Shanghai, your concern for your homeland and your empathy are deeply admired. You have always been enthusiastic about public welfare and relief efforts. I am incompetent and of little ability, and I have encountered this great disaster, and I feel guilty for my inability to comfort the people. Therefore, I am reporting the findings of my investigation to you, hoping that you will raise a large sum of money so that the helpless disaster victims in the entire county can have hope for relief and the coastal dikes can be repaired as soon as possible. Your great virtue will be a blessing to the entire county."

The World Red Swastika Society telegraphed the Southeast Headquarters of the Red Swastika Society in Shanghai on the 27th to report the situation. The original telegram is recorded below:

Hua County: According to a telegram from the Hua County Relief Branch, "Unfortunately, our county has suffered a devastating flood in the Wei River. The water level suddenly rose to over ten feet, with turbulent waves and an overwhelming force. Nearby areas within a hundred li have become a waterlogged area, sweeping away all lives, property, houses, and graves. Hundreds of people have been killed or injured, and countless livestock have been lost. Over a hundred households have been flooded, especially in Xiaozhangtan, Qinjiatan, Wujiaqiao, and Shilinzhen, where the disaster is most severe. Where the water reaches, steel sand covers the fields, ranging from ten feet deep to several feet shallow. Not only have all the autumn crops been submerged, but even the large trees are half-buried in the sand. The fertile fields have been turned into deserts. Moreover, outside this flood-affected area, various places have also suffered from drought, and all the autumn crops are withered, with little hope of bearing fruit. Tens of thousands of disaster victims are crying out in hunger and cold, which is truly heartbreaking. We hope that benevolent gentlemen and charitable organizations will show great compassion and generously donate relief to save the disaster victims from the water and fire. We eagerly await your response."

Dali County: "On the 8th of last month, sudden wind and rain caused the Luo and Wei Rivers to flood, turning the villages along the banks into waterlogged areas. Eight or nine out of ten disaster victims were soaked, and only one or two out of a hundred personal belongings were salvaged. Dozens of villages have become valleys, and hundreds of disaster victims are crying out in hunger and cold, their voices echoing across the land. It is truly unbearable to witness or hear. Upon investigation, over thirty villages have been flooded, with over 122,000 mu of autumn fields affected, over a hundred people killed or injured, dozens of livestock lost, over 1,340 houses collapsed, and personal belongings lost with a value of over 107,300 yuan, totaling over one million yuan. It is truly a rare disaster unseen in a century. As autumn turns to winter, tens of thousands of disaster victims will inevitably freeze and starve to death. We earnestly request your society to witness the imminent danger and have compassion, and to promptly allocate a large sum of relief funds to save these disaster victims from this dire situation."

Dredging of Sanlintang Port in Pudong 142

Establishment of a Dredging Committee

Sanlintang Port in Pudong, Shanghai County, is the main river of the county, spanning the border of Nanhui County. Recently, due to years of disrepair, the riverbed has become almost level with the land, not only causing irrigation difficulties and transportation disruptions but also posing problems for firefighting and drinking water. The Fourth District Office of the County, in view of this, believes that if measures are not taken to dredge the river as soon as possible, the future is unimaginable. Therefore, the District Chief, Fu Dianying, reported the situation to the County Government and requested that Nanhui County jointly handle the matter. Therefore, the District Office specially convened the Chambers of Commerce and Security Regiments of the two counties of Shangnan, as well as the relevant district, township, and town chiefs along the river, to discuss the dredging. A meeting was held the day before yesterday to establish a Dredging Committee. The charter was immediately approved, and Shen Shuzhuang, Yao Jiasheng, Fu Dianying, Huo Xusheng, and thirteen others were elected as members.

Joint Water-Land Transportation Between Kunshan and Changshu on the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway 143

To Be Implemented from October 1

The Shanghai-Nanjing Railway has been actively developing joint water-land transportation in recent years. Recently, it signed a joint transportation contract for passengers, luggage, and parcels with the Yuanyi Steamboat Bureau of Hupu Town, a coastal town in Changshu County, for travel between Qingyang Port Station and Hupu. The main points of the agreement are as follows: (Fare) Shanghai North Station to Qingyang Port: 1.30 yuan for second class, 0.65 yuan for third class, and 0.35 yuan for fourth class. Qingyang Port to Hupu: a flat rate of 0.35 yuan. (Luggage Freight) If the free weight limit is exceeded, a fee of 0.15 yuan will be charged for every 20 kilograms or fraction thereof. (Parcel Freight) Shanghai North to Qingyang Port: 0.007 silver yuan per kilogram, with a minimum charge of 0.20 yuan per piece. Qingyang Port to Hupu: 0.20 silver yuan per 60 kilograms or fraction thereof. (Commission) If the railway's revenue from this joint transportation is less than 5,000 yuan per month, a commission of 1.5% will be given. If it is above 5,000 yuan, a commission of 3% will be given, but no commission will be given for revenue from joint transportation tickets sold by the railway. (Settlement) The joint transportation business will be reported and settled by both parties monthly. (Termination) If the steamboat bureau transfers part or all of the joint transportation business rights to a third party without the written permission of the railway bureau, or if the steamboat bureau violates the railway bureau's regulations, the railway bureau may cancel the contract at any time. The contract stipulates that it will be implemented from October 1st of this year and will be valid for one year. If both parties agree upon expiration, it will be extended.

Two Railway Bureaus Issue Bills of Lading 144

Their Nature Is as Valuable Securities

Having the Same Value as Goods

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce recently received a letter from the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus, stating: "It has been a long-standing practice for cargo merchants to use railway-issued freight receipts to handle exchange settlements after entrusting the railway to transport goods in order to circulate funds. However, these freight receipts are only vouchers for cargo merchants to pick up goods from the railway and cannot be equated with valuable securities. Therefore, after the railway implemented responsible transportation, it specially ordered a type of voucher called the 'Bill of Lading' for the convenience of cargo merchants handling exchange settlements for reported goods. Its nature has the same value as the goods (as a valuable security) and is specifically for cargo merchants to handle borrowing, lending, or trading. All the articles of association and handling rules were promulgated and implemented by the Ministry of Railways in July of last year. As for the procedures for applying for a bill of lading, cargo merchants only need to indicate 'Please issue a bill of lading' in the 'Special Matters' column of the consignment note when filling out the consignment note for entrusting the railway to transport goods, and the railway can do so accordingly. The matter is very simple, and the benefits are very extensive. Fearing that the various forwarding companies may not fully understand the use of this bill of lading, we request that your association forward this notice to promote it as much as possible. Please handle it accordingly."

The Dispute Over Wage Increase Demands by Fresh Pork Industry Workers Resolved 147

Both Parties Signed Ten Conditions

The dispute over the demands by workers in the fresh pork industry in Nanshi to revise the conditions and increase wages was mediated by the Social Affairs Bureau three times. Except for the wage item, both parties agreed to resolve the remaining clauses. The dispute over the issue of wage increases was very fierce. Some workers previously declared a strike because they believed that the capitalists were insincere. The union sent personnel to persuade them to resume work and await mediation. The Social Affairs Bureau was deeply afraid of the expansion of the dispute, so it convened another mediation yesterday. Shen Genshou and Wang Ayin represented the labor side, and Xin Wenyao and Xu Youdi represented the capital side. Dai Youheng of the Municipal Party Department was also present. The meeting was chaired by Pei Yan of the Third Section, and Wang Zhiqin recorded the minutes. First, the chairman consulted the opinions of both parties. After a long period of consultation, it was decided to increase wages by two yuan for those earning below ten yuan, one yuan and twenty cents for those earning below twenty yuan, and one yuan for those earning above twenty yuan. Both parties were satisfied and signed thirteen clauses, announcing that the mediation was successful.

Reactions to the Telephone Price Increase Again 148

Letter from the Nanjing Road Citizens Association to the Taxpayers Association

The Shanghai Nanjing Road Businessmen's Association and the First District Branch of the Citizens' Association strongly opposed the Shanghai Telephone Company's price increase in the past. Now that the company has news of another price increase, the association has sent another letter to the Chinese Taxpayers Association to express their opposition. The original letter reads: "Recently, Shanghai newspapers have published news that the Shanghai Telephone Company has news of another price increase. Once the Shanghai Municipal Council approves it, the measures will be announced. The telephone is a public transportation undertaking and should be extremely cheap to benefit citizens. Last year, the Shanghai Telephone Company, based on a report by Mr. Anson, which is not suitable for Shanghai's social and economic conditions, and with dubious requests, was rashly approved by the Shanghai Municipal Council to increase prices retroactively to March 27th of the same year, which caused opposition from users. The authorities disregarded this matter so rudely, and users had to reluctantly pay under protest. The case is still pending. However, the company arbitrarily speculated that users had already reached an agreement and then increased prices again in no time, and the measures were not announced in advance, allowing them to do whatever they wanted, which is not the means that a public utility operator should take. Your association is the highest authority for taxpayers in the district and must have been prepared long ago. The failure of the taxpayers' opposition to the telephone price increase last time was due to the fact that various industries with the most users sat back and watched, hoping to reap the benefits of others. However, your association's attitude was too peaceful, and it cannot be spared from criticism. Looking at Shanghai's business, the peace of the Pacific Ocean is threatened by the violence of the Japanese, causing unease among the people. The rural areas of the interior are declining, and there is a lack of purchasing power. Over the years, there has only been decline and no revival. However, the Shanghai Municipal Council, at a meeting of taxpayers, decided not to increase donations this year, but increased all license donations as much as possible. Although the land and house donation rates did not change, their prices were overestimated to implement the donation increase. However, this can still be hoped that the public will use it for taxpayers, and it is only inconsistent with financial principles. As for public utilities, how should the Shanghai Municipal Council protect taxpayers so that they can use them cheaply? In fact, this purpose has not been achieved. The water company agreed to the water company's amendment to the contract, allowing it to increase prices arbitrarily, causing taxpayers to pay a lot of money. The electricity company allowed price increases due to coal prices, but did not order price reductions when coal prices fell. The streetcars and public buses are also the same. It is well known that the authorities have no regard for taxpayers. The Shanghai Telephone Company is taking advantage of this weakness and naturally dares to increase prices again and again and continue to try. The contract can be ignored, and the mutual agreement in the 30th year of the Republic of China can be ignored. In short, all the provisions in the contract that are beneficial to taxpayers are despised by the Shanghai Municipal Council or allowed to be changed. The provisions that are beneficial to public utility companies are vigorously maintained by the Shanghai Municipal Council, and the public opinion of the citizens is disregarded. If this is not fought for, how can it become a city? Therefore, we urgently and directly state this matter, hoping that you will investigate it, seriously negotiate, and not repeat the mistakes of the past. We sincerely hope for public cooperation."

Jiangshun Steamer Harrassment by Inspection in Zhenjiang 149

Boarding for Drug Inspection

Hindering the Steamer's Voyage

-China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Submits Report Requesting Strict Prohibition-

The Jiangshun steamer, belonging to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, was traveling from Hankou to Shanghai. Upon arriving in Zhenjiang, individuals claiming to be members of a drug inspection team boarded the vessel to conduct an inspection, preventing its departure. Furthermore, they directed the local security force to stage a demonstration against the steamer, creating a serious situation. The on-board military police detained the individuals, who were later released after mediation. The company has now submitted a report to the authorities, requesting that officials investigate and prohibit such actions. The true details of this incident are reported as follows:

Drug Inspection: The Jiangshun steamer of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company was returning to Shanghai from Hankou. Upon arriving in Zhenjiang, the ship docked and began loading cargo. Suddenly, several individuals in plainclothes boarded the ship, claiming to be a drug inspection team and demanding to search the Jiangshun steamer. The crew allowed them to search the various cabins, crew quarters, and tea rooms. No contraband was found. By this time, the ship's cargo was loaded, and the captain ordered the anchor to be raised. However, the inspection team insisted on searching the cargo hold and refused to allow the Jiangshun to depart, causing a major disturbance on board. The crew, aware that the ship had a strict schedule that could not be delayed, advised the team to disembark. However, a portion of the inspection team went ashore and summoned a large number of security guards, using force to prevent the ship's departure. The situation quickly descended into chaos.

Three Arrested: The Capital Military Police Headquarters of the Yangtze River Naval Patrol had assigned six military police officers to the steamer to protect the voyage. Hearing of the dispute in the hold, the military police and escort police officers went to investigate. They argued that since no contraband had been found on board, there was no reason to hinder or delay the ship's departure. The military police officers urged the inspection team to go ashore, but they refused and instead clashed with the officers. Considering the inspection team's unreasonable behavior and obstruction of traffic, the military police officers detained the three leaders of the inspection team. The incident was immediately reported to the Public Security Bureau, which dispatched officers to the steamer. After hearing the crew's account of the situation, the bureau officers mediated the situation and ordered the military police officers to release the three detained inspectors. At the same time, the inspectors were ordered to issue a letter of reconciliation, which was signed by both parties to conclude the matter.

Disturbance in Tongzhou: After the Jiangshun steamer departed from Zhenjiang, it was hoped that it would be able to proceed peacefully. However, the inspectors were apparently still bitter and sent a telegram from Zhenjiang to the Tongzhou security force, instructing them to detain the Jiangshun steamer upon its arrival and prevent it from passing through. As a result, when the Jiangshun arrived in Tongzhou, the local security force was on the riverbank, aiming their guns at the ship as if preparing to fire. The passengers on board, unaware of the situation, were terrified. The Tongzhou agency office inquired about the cause of the situation and reported it to the county government. The county government sent officials to the scene to explain the true nature of the inspectors' instigation and disturbance to the security force, advising the guards not to engage in such actions and to withdraw. The captain of the Jiangshun steamer (a Westerner), seeing many armed men on the shore aiming guns at the ship in a threatening manner, also took out his own handgun, preparing to return fire. The security guards on the riverbank then fled in a panic, and the ship was able to depart for Shanghai.

Reported to the Authorities for Strict Prohibition: Recently, various company steamers traveling downstream to Shanghai have frequently been subjected to harassment by self-proclaimed drug inspection teams in the Zhenjiang and Tongzhou area. These teams board the ships to conduct searches and engage in various forms of abuse. Most of these team members are in plainclothes and do not wear uniforms. Some have even beaten the tea room attendants and stokers, and this has happened more than once. Jardine Matheson's steamer has even had to deal with the situation. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's steamers have also been disturbed several times. Yesterday, the company reported the situation to the authorities, requesting an investigation into the existence of such a drug inspection team and urging strict prohibition to ensure the safety of travelers and the maintenance of the shipping industry.

Shanghai Search for Murderer in Dalian Suitcase Case 150

But No Clues to Be Found

A Dentsu dispatch from Osaka on the 28th reports that, according to local newspapers, Dr. Kodama has confessed to being an accessory in the Dalian suitcase murder case. He stated that at 9 p.m. that night, Nakazono and Aoyagi, along with Aoyagi's wife, Ms. Katsumi, went to a dance hall. Nakazono saw Aoyagi and Ms. Katsumi being very intimate and began arguing in the dance hall. Because they were in a public place, they did not make too much of a scene and went together to Dr. Kodama's house. They continued arguing in front of Kodama. Despite his attempts to dissuade them, they did not listen. Aoyagi demanded an apology from Nakazono, but Nakazono refused, and they began fighting. Nakazono, in a fit of anger, fought violently and eventually killed Aoyagi. Kodama could not bear to watch and helped Nakazono commit the crime, cutting up the body, packing it in a suitcase, and transporting it to Ms. Yokoyama's house to hide. Ms. Yokoyama knew about the crime and hid the body. Nakazono and Ms. Katsumi fled Dalian. Kodama stated that he had been unwilling to reveal the truth until now out of concern for his reputation and position. However, the matter has come to this point, and he has no choice but to tell the truth. The Osaka Police Department firmly believes that the murderer is still hiding in Osaka and today mobilized 16 armed commandos to lie in wait at Osaka Station. Any male and female passengers found sitting on the same chair in a passenger car are questioned about their origin if they do not have business cards. It is said that many newlyweds have been inconvenienced, and jokes have been made everywhere.

The Continental Daily reports that, after the suitcase murder case was discovered in Dalian three days ago, it was said that the murderer Nakazono had left Dalian and might have come to Shanghai. Therefore, the police of the Japanese Consulate General in this city yesterday searched everywhere for Nakazono's whereabouts, but no clues have been found. It is currently suspected that Nakazono may have returned to Japan to make it easier to hide. However, as of last night, the Japanese Consulate in this city had not received any information from its home country regarding Nakazono's whereabouts. The Japanese community in this city is paying close attention to this case due to its bizarre circumstances. According to information from Dalian, the deceased Aoyagi and the suspect Nakazono were both lovers of Dr. Kodama's wife, who was the director of the pathology department at the South Manchuria Railway Hospital. They even fought in front of Kodama and his wife. After Nakazono killed Aoyagi, he dismembered the body, placed it in a suitcase, and moved it to the house of his former lover, Ms. Yokoyama. Twenty days later, the authorities discovered the body, arrested Ms. Yokoyama, and learned the details of the case. They immediately sent out telegrams to arrest the suspects. It is said that Kodama's wife, a key figure in the case, fled to Japan after the incident and is expected to be apprehended soon.

Detailed Account of the Jianghai Customs Clerk Embezzlement Case Trial 151

Judge Opens Preliminary Hearing Yesterday Due to Complex Facts

Defendants Mostly Shirk Responsibility and Deny Everything

Su Kunian Wears Short Cloth Coat, Looking Like a Shop Assistant

Presiding Judge Says Su Normally Rides in Cars and Lives Lavishly

-Four Hours of Interrogation, Overcrowded Gallery-

Jianghai Customs clerks and Ningbo native Su Kunian organized the "Huatou" United Company at No. 3 Hankou Road, colluding with customs brokers from foreign firms to forge Jianghai Customs declarations. The clerks then secretly replaced the genuine declarations, embezzling large amounts of customs duties, amounting to tens of thousands of yuan. Shu Bo, Deputy Commissioner of Customs of the Jianghai Customs Anti-Smuggling Department, discovered the fraud and notified the Water Police Department. Chief Inspector Peng Shi and Chinese Detective Cheng Yongnian investigated and confirmed the details, leading to a raid on the company and the arrest of Su Kunian, clerks Shi Cunqiao, Wang Yueren, Wei Anxiang, Jiang Zhenhai, Zhang Songtao, Sun Guozhang, Chen Zhongshan, and Chen Guoliang, a customs broker from the China Soap Company, as well as seven other fugitives, including Han Jincai, who are currently wanted. Prosecutor Ouyang Shu investigated and confirmed the details, and filed a public prosecution for forgery of official documents and embezzlement of national taxes. Su Kunian was also found to be a habitual offender and will be prosecuted more severely. Yesterday afternoon at 1:30 p.m., Qian Chengjun, Presiding Judge of the Criminal Court, opened the third courtroom for the trial. The defendants hired defense attorneys Qu Yue, Jin Yu, and Zhang Enbin, while the Customs hired attorney Jiang Yiping as their agent for the attached civil suit. Because this case is a rare major case, the gallery was overcrowded. The presiding judge ordered the defendants and witnesses Peng Shi and Shu Bo to the court, and then announced that due to the complexity of the facts, a preliminary hearing would be held first.

First, Peng Shi, 42 years old, British, Criminal Chief of the Water Police, resident of the Pudong Customs Warehouse, was questioned. "How was this case discovered?" He replied, "By the Commissioner of Customs of the Anti-Smuggling Section of the Customs." "What was discovered?" He replied, "Customs documents and declarations were stolen, and fake ones were used to replace the real ones." "How many declarations were lost?" He replied, "When it was discovered, we found that a real one had been replaced with a fake one, and the real one was found during a search of the United Company on Sanma Road." "What was declared?" He replied, "A car." "What was the estimated value?" He replied, "I don't remember the exact amount." The official ordered the evidence to be examined and two real and fake declarations were presented. He stated, "The fake one was found at the Customs, and the real one was found by the First Special District Court during a search of the United Company." "Are there any other real or fake declarations?" He replied, "There are many other items that were copied by the United Company. After we, the police, copied them, we handed them over to the Customs for their own investigation." Peng Shi only knew about the car incident; the Customs Commissioner of Customs was more clear about the details. "Which section is in charge of the declarations?" He replied, "It goes through several places, so I can't be sure."

"Who is in charge of the declaration?" He replied that it goes through a couple of different places, he couldn't be sure. The judge then questioned Shu Bo, 36 years old, Norwegian, Deputy Customs Officer of the Anti-Smuggling Division, resident at No. 139 Rue Grorosa, French Concession. "How long have you been in this position?" He replied, "Only six months." "How did you know about the tax evasion?" He replied, "It is our specialized duty." "How did you first find out?" He replied, "We investigated merchants and suspected that there were irregularities at the United Company at No. 3 Hankou Road." "Did you go to the search?" He replied, "I did not go." "When was it?" He replied, "July 20th." "How many real and fake declarations did you find?" He replied, "I don't remember exactly, but everything we found was sent to your court. The first thing we discovered was a car declaration on the printing platform, and the real one was found in the United Company." At this point, the judge questioned Kunian, 26 years old, from Zhenhai, an employee of the United Company and an export broker, resident at No. 4 Huixing Lane, Xihuade Road. "Who opened the United Company?" He replied, "Shao Pengfei opened it." "How many people opened it?" He replied, "One person." "What do you do there?" "I help with export goods." "How long have you been doing it?" He replied, "Two months." "You previously stated that you were an assistant." He replied, "I did not say that." "The crime is not about the employee or assistant, and the statement has your fingerprint. Are you friends with Wang Xiangwen and Jiang Wenyi, whom the court has previously dealt with?" He replied, "Yes, I am." The judge said, "It can be seen that you are habitually unlawful and cannot be forgiven. You committed the same crime with them before, but were not punished, so you went to the United Company to do unlawful things again." He replied, "I only went for a few months." The judge said, "In short, your crimes are irrefutable. You should tell the truth, and perhaps there is a possibility of leniency. What did the boss ask you to do?" He replied, "Send letters." "Where to?" "To the Customs." "To whom?" "Sometimes to Ji Cunqiao, sometimes to Jiang Zhenhai, and the others I can't remember at the moment." "How many times a month do you forge Customs declarations?" He replied, "I don't know." "How many times do you send letters?" He replied, "Two or three times a month." "You previously said that you and the Customs clerks and customs brokers from the foreign firms organized a group to steal blank declarations, fill them out, and send them in." He replied, "I was beaten and could not say anything." The judge said, "You think that you are wearing a short cloth coat today, looking like a shop assistant, but this court has long been aware of your acts of misconduct and extravagance in taking cars on weekdays. You should tell the truth, and the court may be able to show mercy. How did you replace the real declarations with fake ones?" He replied, "I don't know." "If you don't know, how did you point out these eight people as being involved and say that the company gets 10%, the clerks get 25%, and the customs brokers get 35%? These are things that cannot be fabricated." He replied, "I couldn't help it. I said it because I was beaten." "According to what you said today, Shi Cunqiao and Jiang Zhenhai are already ironclad cases. How many times have you handled them?" He replied, "None." "This kind of case is not a case of theft, perhaps it was a coerced confession. How would you understand this kind of thing if you hadn't experienced it? Therefore, if the confession does not match the facts, it can also be declared innocent. But your confession matches the facts. In any case, it is difficult to escape the law. If you can tell the truth, perhaps your intentions can be forgiven and you can be treated with leniency. But now you are just trying to be cunning, which shows that your intentions are evil. So the fault lies with you, the most important person. Moreover, you confessed to the prosecutor that the boss, Shao Pengfei, asked me to commit fraud at the Customs. Did people fabricate this confession?" He replied, "I did not say that." "Which foreign firms did your United Company report?" He replied, "Baohe Foreign Firm." "Not just one?" He replied, "My boss's private affairs, I don't know." "You previously said that it was Meizuishi, Kaili, Yuxingxiang, Xincheng, and many other firms, why not today?" "The prosecutor saw it on the register and recorded it." "This is your confession, where is this kind of thing? Therefore, the co-defendants Xia Lanfang and your brother Su Kangnian, etc., are all people you claimed were apprentices, who did not know the content and were acquitted. You acquitted your comrades, still want to be cunning?" "You also said that on July 14th, Ruirui imported 280 cars." He replied, "I did not say that." "How did you get to know Chen Guoliang?" He replied, "I have never seen him." "You often eat at that restaurant on Fourth Avenue." He replied, "Jiya." The judge said, "Are you such an extravagant and meticulous shop assistant? And you, Shi Cunqiao, Wei Anxiang, etc., eat at which restaurant?" He replied, "I don't know." The judge said, "Since you went to the restaurant, there is no reason not to know. You are just being cunning. Who did you eat with this time?" He replied, "The Baohe Foreign Firm, Mr. Gu." The judge then reprimanded Su severely and ordered him to be taken down, and then questioned Shi Cunqiao, 23 years old, from Yin County, a clerk at the Customs Evaluation Office, resident at No. 10 Shanlong Lane, Quanjia'an Road, Diswei Road. "How long have you been working?" He replied, "One year and two months. I used to be a messenger for the shipowner." "What year did you start working?" He replied, "1930." The judge then reprimanded him angrily, "You are Chinese, you are just a clerk, and you have forgotten your roots and even forgotten your own year? What year is the Republic of China?" He replied, "The Republic of China is the 20th year." "How much is your monthly salary?" He replied, "37 yuan." "How did you get to know Su Kunian and Shao Pengfei?" He replied, "I don't know them." "Are you still working as a clerk?" He replied, "Yes, I am." "Are you in charge of the declarations at the Evaluation Office?" He replied, "There are five of us, I am only in charge of small verifications." "On the 17th, did you go to the Hezuo Company with Wang Yueren and Wei Anxiang?" He replied, "No, I did not go." "What did you say in front of the prosecutor?" He replied, "The prosecutor copied the statement from the Water Police Department." The judge then shouted in shock and scolded, "There is no such thing, it is obviously cunning." He replied, "The Water Police Department forced me to confess." "Why didn't you report the injury at the time?" He replied, "I was already scared by the instruments of torture before I was beaten." The judge said, "This is obviously nonsense. You also said that Su Kunian gave you 1,800 yuan on the 17th, and you three split it, each getting 600 yuan. This is in the prosecutor's confession, you can't deny it." At this point, Wang Yueren, 26 years old, from Shanghai, Jianghai Customs clerk, resident at No. 40 Hongqiao, was questioned. "I am a clerk at the import inspection platform, I don't know Su Kunian." "Which department does the inspection platform belong to?" He replied, "The General Affairs Department." "What does it do?" He replied, "It fills in the tax silver on the blank declarations." "Are you familiar with Wei Anxiang and Shi Cunqiao?" He replied, "Yes, I am." "What did you do at the Hezuo Company on the 17th?" He replied, "I didn't go." "Why did Shi Cunqiao confess you?" He replied, "There is no such thing." "Did you steal the declaration or did Shi steal it?" He replied, "I didn't steal it." "You got one hundred yuan, did you get eaten by someone? How long have you been doing it?" He replied, "I didn't do it." "You previously confessed that you, Wei Anxiang, and Shi Cunqiao received a total of 1,800 yuan, don't deny it. Who initiated it, did Su Kunian come to seduce you?" He replied, "We did not say, the prosecutor only asked for our names and ages, and did not ask anything else." The judge said, "You are spreading this kind of rumor, there is no such thing, you are all cunning traitors." At this point, Wei Anxiang, 26 years old, from Shanghai, resident at No. 6 Anping Lane, Fangbang Road, Nanyang Bridge, was questioned. "I am a clerk on the third floor of the Customs, I have been there for three and a half years, and my monthly salary is 37 yuan." "Do you know Shi Cunqiao and Wang Yueren?" He replied, "I know them." "Are you on good terms?" He replied, "Yes, we are." "How many of you stole the declaration?" He replied, "I don't know." "How did you previously confess that Wang Yueren went to steal, and you kept watch?" He replied, "I said that after the Water Police threatened me." "How did you confess at the Prosecutor's Office?" He replied, "The prosecutor copied the confession from the police station." At this point, the judge questioned Jiang Zhenhai, also known as Jiang Zhenhan, 30 years old, from Yancheng, resident at No. 28 Xiangguang Lane, Xihuade Road, formerly a clerk on the third floor of the Customs, who stopped working on May 30th of this year. "When were you arrested by the Water Police?" He replied, "Sometime in July, I was sick at home." "Who are you familiar with?" He replied, "I am most familiar with Wei Anxiang, the rest are just colleagues." "When did you meet Su Kunian?" He replied, "One day, the Chinese secretary of the Commissioner of Customs, Mr. Wu Xirong, asked me to send a letter to the Evaluation Office, where I met him." "So Su often comes?" He replied, "I don't know." "He asked you to take the declaration?" He replied, "I am only sending letters." "How did Shi Cunqiao confess that you were involved?" He replied, "During the Shanghai War, he said that I, a native of Jiangbei, was a traitor, and I said that he, a native of Ningbo, was a real traitor, so we fought. He deliberately framed me out of hatred." "Did Shi Cunqiao ever bite you, or did you admit it yourself? And you introduced Wei Anxiang and Su Kunian, because he asked you to steal, but the declaration did not pass through your hands, so you introduced Wei into it." He replied, "This was also bitten by Shi Cunqiao." At this point, Zhang Qiutao, 36 years old, from Nanhui, resident at No. 26 Yongzhen Lane, Gongyi Pier, Jianghai Customs clerk on the second floor, who is in charge of ordering tax bills, was questioned. "The staff will hand it down after ordering the tax bill, and we will send it to the tax registration desk after ordering it. Where does it end up?" He replied, "The printing platform." "What station do you manage?" He replied, "The starting station, Chen Zhongshan manages the tax registration desk." "How long have you been working?" He replied, "Twenty years." "You stole the declaration?" He replied, "I don't know, I was truly wronged. How did it involve me?" He replied, "That's really strange." "Do you know Shao Pengfei?" He replied, "I don't know him." "Do you know Han Jincai?" He replied, "Yes, he used to be a colleague." "What was he doing at your house that day?" He replied, "My sister-in-law was suing, I didn't see him." "What about Su Kunian?" He replied, "One day, Su was wearing black clothes, like a rogue, at 4:30 in the afternoon, when office hours had ended, he stood by the starting station, I thought he was a thief stealing things, so I questioned him and there was a conflict, so he bore a grudge and bit me." At this point, Sun Guozhang, 27 years old, from Nantong, resident at No. 19 Deming Lane, Dongpushe Road, Jianghai Customs clerk on the fourth floor, was questioned. "I specialize in writing declaration numbers." "Who orders the declarations?" He replied, "Wan Shougen." "How many orders at a time?" He replied, "One order per ship name." "How did you get to know Su Kunian?" He replied, "I met him in the waiting room a month ago." "Is there any connection between you and stealing the declaration?" He replied, "No, my declaration is already ordered and completed, and it cannot be torn off. Which section are you in?" He replied, "The document management room of the General Affairs Section, which is the last place." At this point, Chen Zhongshan, 33 years old, from Nanhui, resident at No. 25 Yuyuan Lane, XinJia Road, Jianghai Customs clerk on the first floor, was questioned. "Are you more familiar with Sun Guozhang or other people?" He replied, "The same." "What about Zhang Qiutao and you?" He replied, "We work at the same desk. What does the starting station do?" He replied, "Send the bill to the tax registration desk. I don't know Su Kunian, but one day at 4:30 in the afternoon, he was at the starting station and asked the supervisory station to collect tax silver, but it was too late, so I had a conflict." The judge said, "You were also implicated by Su Kunian." At this point, Chen Guoliang, 25 years old, from Chuansha, a customs broker from the China Soap Company, resident at No. 295 Weihaiwei Road, was questioned. "How did you get to know Chen Amao?" He replied, "He used to be a customs broker, he quit last year, and I took over." "Do you know Su Kunian?" He replied, "I don't know him." "Was he introduced by Chen Amao?" He replied, "I have never seen this person." "This is your original confession, this has nothing to do." He replied, "The introduction is an introduction, but I don't know what he does." "Where are the 600 barrels of Duxiang from?" He replied, "From the company." "How much tax was paid?" He replied, "More than 3,000 yuan." "Did you pay the Customs with a check?" He replied, "I took the customs bill, drew a check, and sent it to the Customs, and it was reported to the Maotai Foreign Firm. "You said earlier that Chen Amao reported it on your behalf." He replied, "When I went, it was 3:30, and Amao said it was too late, so he took it to the upper floor for me." "What year did you pay him 400 yuan?" He replied, "He borrowed it from my father." At this point, the judge ordered a retrial at a later date, and the defendants were taken back into custody. It was already 5:30.

Zhang Lexuan Specialized in Abortion for Women 153

Don't Know How Many Fetuses Have Been Harmed

Truly a Scourge to the People

-Zhang Himself Is on the Run, His Assistant Is Detained-

Zhang Lexuan, who lives at No. 250 Hankou Road, claims to be proficient in Huangdi's medical skills, especially good at performing abortions for women. Therefore, the abortion medical fees he charges are fixed amounts, based on the length of pregnancy. For example, if the pregnancy is only one month, the fee is five yuan; two months, ten yuan, and so on, rarely increasing or decreasing easily. If the aborted woman requires a guarantee that there will be no danger to her life, then the fees he charges are not fixed, depending on the person. For wealthy families, he demands exorbitant prices, but the lowest price is no less than two or three hundred gold. Since Zhang has used his skills to practice medicine, he has harmed an unknown number of fetuses, truly a scourge to the people and a scorpion of society. Recently, his secret was discovered by Xu Zexin, a detective from the Laozha Police Station, who wanted to collect evidence of his crimes and specially visited a pregnant woman, Ms. Lin, and ordered her to try it first. On the 7th of this month, Ms. Lin quietly went alone and arrived at his clinic, where she was received by Liu Gongwei, a Ningbo native hired by Zhang as an assistant. After Liu asked about her purpose, he went into the room and called Zhang out. Zhang first examined the woman's pulse and then said to the woman that the fetus in her belly was already five months old. If it needs to be aborted, each month will be charged five yuan, totaling 15 yuan. Ms. Lin then asked if she could be guaranteed no danger after the abortion, and Zhang said that abortion is painless, but if insurance is required, the medical expenses should be 200 yuan. Ms. Lin then pretended to say that the price was too high, and that she would consider it again and leave. Two days later, she returned to discuss the price, and Zhang reduced it to 18 yuan. Ms. Lin paid ten yuan first, obtained the medicinal powder, medicinal water, and the receipt written by Zhang, which included a guarantee of no danger, and handed it all over to Detective Xu, who turned it over to the police chief. Since the evidence was complete, the matter should be strictly investigated. He also ordered the detective to rush to arrest him yesterday, but Zhang had keen ears and fled when he heard the news. Only Liu Gongwei, who assisted in the abortion, was taken back to the police station and detained. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Special District Local Court, where he was interrogated by Judge Zhan Liangce. After the police lawyer Zhang Shizhu stated the circumstances, he also stated that the medicine and powder obtained by the woman had been chemically examined and were all fake medicines. Therefore, the defendant was actually committing fraud, not just performing abortions, and should be severely punished. Ms. Lin was also brought to the case to testify to everything. When questioned, Liu confessed, "I originally worked at the Zuolin Hospital opened by Li Zuolin, but I was invited by Zhang to assist. Now Zhang has escaped," and so on. Judge Zhan then ordered the defendant to be detained and set a later date for further interrogation.

Japanese Yarn Passing Off as Domestic Goods: Ten Factories Vigorously Avoid Litigation 155

Fearing Legal Sanctions, They Seek Reconciliation with Influential Figures

Yesterday, after Lengthy Negotiations, a Fine Was Paid to Assist in Disaster Relief

Whether There Are Other Understandings on Shenxin's Side Remains Unclear

Whether the Consolidated Tax Office Will Pursue the Matter is Key to the Case

Ten factories, including Gong Zu, recently reported the transport of Japanese yarn as domestic goods to the Consolidated Tax Office of the Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui region. The bureau discovered this and notified Shenxin Factory No. 5. Consequently, the factory filed a criminal self-accusation against Yu Xifan, the manager of the ten factories, in the First Special District Court. Recently, those ten factories, including Yu Xifan, Chen Zhongxian, Wang Liwei, Sun Xizu, Yu Yuxin, Zhou Songmao, Chai Zhixiang, Zhao Bingnan, Wang Gensheng, and Guan Bingqing, fearing that once involved in litigation, they would inevitably be subject to national law, spent their days seeking reconciliation everywhere and making great efforts to cover up the matter to avoid being abandoned by the public. The details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now known that yesterday, Zhang Zilian, Ge Shengru, and Zhu Wenqi came forward to invite the parties involved and mediators to meet at the Atlantic Vegetable Club. After four hours of private discussions, Shenxin expressed its acceptance of the reconciliation. It is rumored that the compensation from the ten factories to Shenxin will be used to provide funds to the Yellow River Flood Disaster Relief Society. Afterwards, reporters inquired with Sun Zuji, the plaintiff's lawyer, about the mediation process. He stated that it was indeed the case. When asked about the compensation for Factories No. 5 and No. 9, he said that it had not been discussed. When asked whether the two parties had signed any agreements, he said that it was only a verbal agreement. Therefore, whether the matter will be resolved so simply is still unclear, and we will continue to investigate and record. As for some people saying that the ten factories' act of passing off Shenxin's products as their own is now a fait accompli, and if Shenxin insists on compensation for past losses, the ten factories will inevitably go bankrupt, these are all one-sided arguments. The fact that the ten factories took such a great risk and were discovered, even leading to legal action, proves the crimes of these unscrupulous merchants. It is even more difficult to allow them to escape the law in order to warn others in the future. Therefore, if the ten factories were to go bankrupt as a result, they would deserve it. At the same time, Shenxin's acceptance of the reconciliation is unwise. As for the Consolidated Tax Office, it was the first to discover the case. To maintain the prestige of the national authority, it is currently collecting evidence and preparing to punish the ten factories for their due crimes. Therefore, the future outcome of the case, and whether the unscrupulous merchants will be subject to legal sanctions, depends entirely on the attitude of the Consolidated Tax Office.

The Two Courts of the First Special District Prohibit Giving Tips to Court Staff 158

Do Not Give Tips to Police Officers and Servants

Those Who Consider It Bribery Will Be Severely Punished If Discovered

Jiangsu High Court Second Branch, Jiangsu Shanghai First Special District Local Court, Proclamation No. 937 states: "Upon investigation, if the process servers of the two courts demand more than the prescribed amount for serving documents, or if the bailiffs and servants solicit tips from litigants, it is a violation of court discipline. We have repeatedly issued proclamations ordering them to be reported at any time for strict punishment. However, it is heard that some litigants are still accustomed to the practices of the former government offices and voluntarily pay extra or give tips even without being solicited, calling it a reward. Little do they know that these police officers and servants are employed by the court and receive corresponding salaries. Their service to the parties involved is a matter of their duty, and the parties involved have no need to reward them. If rewards are given rashly, it will only encourage their non-essential desires. Those who do not give rewards will inevitably harbor thoughts of solicitation, or because of the existence of rewards, the treatment will be clearly divided into thick and thin, which is detrimental to both the public interest and the court discipline. If they receive property for actions in the line of duty, which can be considered bribery, they will be severely punished once discovered and verified. Thickening them will only harm them, and those who offer bribes will also be prosecuted. Therefore, we hereby notify all litigants that they must not give any tips to police officers and servants beyond the prescribed amount. Do not cause inconvenience. Everyone must comply. This is hereby proclaimed. September 23rd, Republic of China 22nd year, Court President Shen Jiayi, Court President Guo Yunguan."

Old Court Badges of the Local Court are Abolished 159

Jiangsu Shanghai Local Court Proclamation No. 386 states: "Regarding the proclamation, upon investigation, the round badges previously issued by this court, with the national emblem in the middle and green and blue on the outside with a red border, and the words 'Jiangsu Shanghai Local Court Badge,' have been replaced by rectangular badges, with half of the blue sky with a white sun on the top and red with white characters on the bottom, and the words 'Shanghai Local Court.' These badges are hereby abolished and will not be worn from this day forward. In order to prevent abuses in the future, badges will not be issued for the time being. For fear of not being fully known, this is hereby proclaimed. September 26th, Republic of China 22nd year, Court President Shen Xiqing, Chief Prosecutor Lou Ying."

Qian Yi Enterprise Silver Company: A Newly Emerging Enterprise 162

Qian Yi Enterprise Silver Company unites the financial, industrial, and engineering sectors to seek benefits for society. It is organized by influential figures in the financial world. After the reorganization, in view of the fact that the financial, industrial, and engineering sectors have never had the opportunity to communicate, it is dedicated to enterprise investment and has formed a technical cooperation committee composed of specialists to support enterprises, improve production, reward inventions, and promote sales. It has also contacted various domestic goods factories to provide a place for experts to implement their abilities. After many days of preparation, it held an inaugural meeting at the company the other day. Those present included Zhuang Zhihuan, Zhi Bingyuan, Lu Chengyao, Li Qianjun, Zhang Yanyu, Huang Bingkui, Wang Shiqiang, Shi Zhaohan, and other well-known engineering experts in China, as well as company directors He Gusheng, Wang Boyuan, Liang Chenlan, Chen Xiaodie, Sun Hegao, and others, forming a unified whole. They are now actively working and will be the hub of the financial, industrial, and engineering sectors to seek social welfare. The articles of association are recorded below:

Design Service Articles of Association: This company, in order to facilitate entrepreneurs or inventors to combine capital and achieve twice the results with half the effort, has established a technical cooperation association, which is divided into twelve types: machinery, chemistry, electricity, ceramics, mining and metallurgy, civil engineering, agriculture and forestry, architecture, cotton weaving, silk weaving, wool weaving, printing and dyeing. The company hires experts to form a technical cooperation committee, which specializes in designing, consulting, and connecting work for the members of the association in order to improve products and increase production. In addition to the technical cooperation and the articles of the technical cooperation committee being determined separately, the design service methods are now specially stipulated as follows: (A) Enterprise Design: (1) Entrepreneurs who are willing to invest a certain amount of capital and hope to receive a certain annual interest rate, who have certain necessary conditions, or who can hold a certain position, may entrust this company in writing to introduce investment in a corresponding enterprise or entrust this company to design it. The company will, within the possible range of its capital strength, plan in detail, select a certain item, and prepare a business budget for inspection. If it is agreeable, the company must sign a contract with the company and extract a percentage of the sales of the product as compensation. The amount of compensation shall be stated in the budget. (2) Entrepreneurs who select a business and want to ensure that the construction of the factory and the equipment are suitable and do not encounter difficulties halfway may entrust this company to undertake the entire design, issue a quotation, and charge a handling fee of 1% to 5% of the total construction cost. As for various projects, whether or not they are contracted by this company, they can be free from restraint. (3) Inventors who research a certain item and feel difficulties in manufacturing and repair due to insufficient capital may entrust this company to review and design their aspirations and their estimated costs in order to assist them in success or introduce them to corresponding entrepreneurs for cooperation. The articles of association, contracts, trademark registration, and company registration can be handled by lawyers and accountants specially contracted by this company. (4) Factories that have already been established and want to improve the original status or work efficiency may entrust this company to design according to their ability and wishes. The design fee is determined according to the size of the factory, business, and simplicity. (5) Factories that want to improve their original products may entrust this company to research, design, and improve them. In addition to charging for labor and material costs, a certain percentage of the excess of future sales over the original amount shall be extracted as compensation for this company. The amount of compensation is also stipulated in the plan. (6) This company unites major factories, such as printing factories, canning factories, and glass factories, to specialize in manufacturing decorations for various factories and businesses in order to obtain high-quality, low-priced, and mutually responsive convenience. All those who are contracted by this company shall be based on the original price, but the commission shall be charged to both the entrusting party and the contracting party at 1%. (7) This company employs advertising talents to specialize in designing publicity matters for various factories, such as advertisements and texts and pictures in newspapers, various publicity in meeting places, broadcasts on radio stations, advertisements on screens in movie theaters or theaters, and all tedious procedures such as daily-use stationery and postal mailings, which can be fully responsible for handling in order to obtain the benefit of low cost and broad effect. (8) This company jointly establishes joint shopping malls in various places with various factories. The articles of association will be determined separately. (9) This company publishes a monthly publication that can be published at any time for inventions or improved industrial products in order to introduce them. The articles of association will be determined separately. (B) Financial Assistance: (10) When entrepreneurs need capital for the development of their enterprises, they can be raised on their behalf after being qualified by the company and collect stock funds on their behalf. (11) Entrepreneurs who lack working capital and want to use all or part of their assets or lend them out on a daily basis can be given assistance after being qualified by the company. (C) Trademark Utilization: (12) The company shall apply for registration as a trademark for exclusive use. If any industrial products invented by the company or improved by the company want to use the company's trademark, 2 to 5 thousandths of the total sales amount of the product shall be extracted as the company's trademark interest. (13) All factories established by the company shall use Qian Yi Enterprise Silver Company Factory No. ○ as their business brand. If entrepreneurs or inventors want to use the company's factory name, they must obtain the company's permission and sign a contract to comply with it, but their profits and losses shall be calculated by each factory and shall not be jointly related to the company. (D) Supplementary Provisions: (14) If there are any deficiencies in these articles of association, they may be amended at any time.

Articles of Association of the Technical Cooperation Committee: (1) Qian Yi Enterprise Silver Company has established a technical cooperation committee to facilitate the joint cooperation of technical experts with the industrial and financial sectors and has hired specialized scholars to organize it. (2) The Technical Cooperation Committee is temporarily divided into the following twelve groups: chemistry, electricity, machinery, civil engineering, architecture, ceramics, agriculture and forestry, mining and metallurgy, cotton spinning, silk weaving, line weaving, printing and dyeing. (3) The Technical Cooperation Committee has a number of members who are responsible for all investigations, research, design, and consulting duties related to the technical cooperation of various enterprises. (4) The Technical Cooperation Committee has three standing committee members who are stationed in Qian Yi Enterprise Silver Company to perform all the tasks of the committee. (5) Each group of the Technical Cooperation Committee appoints a chairman who is responsible for handling all the duties of the group. (6) The members of the Technical Cooperation Committee are temporarily designated as purely voluntary and are appointed by Qian Yi Enterprise Silver Company. (7) The Technical Cooperation Committee holds a regular meeting once a month. When necessary, the standing committee members may convene a temporary meeting. (8) In order to implement the various designs of the Technical Cooperation Committee, Qian Yi Enterprise Silver Company has established the following four departments in its design department at its head office: (A) Investigation, handling the investigation of the circumstances of various enterprises, statistics of price indexes, and other matters. (B) Research, handling the planning and drafting of designs and improvements on industrial enterprises. (C) Consulting, handling technical consultations from the industrial sector and reviewing the designs of successful research or inventors, as well as reviewing the value of real estate and financial property for enterprises as a standard for investment in the financial sector. (D) Introduction, handling the introduction or contribution of successful research results and talents to the industrial sector to solve factory organization and management and production and sales links. (9) When various enterprise organizations that have joined the Technical Cooperation Committee of Qian Yi Enterprise Silver Company request the company to design on its behalf, the design shall be handled by the committee as soon as possible. (10) The proceeds of the Committee members from the use and introduction of research, invention, or improvement achievements by Qian Yi Enterprise Silver Company to the industrial sector shall be disposed of by the Committee. (11) The design fees charged by Qian Yi Enterprise Silver Company to enterprises for the design by the Committee members shall be disposed of by the Committee. (12) If there are any deficiencies in these articles of association, they may be amended at any time.

Articles of Association of the Technical Cooperation Association: (1) All types of enterprise organizations, such as chemical, electrical, mechanical, civil engineering, architectural, ceramic, agricultural and forestry, mining and metallurgical, cotton textile, wool textile, silk textile, and printing and dyeing, may join the association as group members. (2) All technical experts who have corresponding achievements in the above-mentioned various enterprise studies and who have been approved by the Technical Cooperation Committee of this company may join this association as individual members. (3) Group members pay a monthly fee of several yuan. Those who have special sponsorship are listed separately as sponsoring members. Individual members pay an annual fee of 10 yuan. (4) Group members hold a regular meeting once a month, and individual members hold a general meeting once a year. A temporary meeting is convened in case of special circumstances. (5) This association has a number of directors who are appointed by Qian Yi Silver Company from among the members to handle all affairs of the association. (6) Qian Yi Enterprise Silver Company employs lawyers, accountants, chemists, engineers, and advertising specialists who are stationed in the company. All group members of this association are entitled to the following special rights: (1) Any legal affairs that require a lawyer's official letter may be entrusted to the company's lawyers for free handling. (2) Any accounting matters that require an accountant's review may be entrusted to the company's accountants for free handling. (3) Any architectural mechanization matters may be entrusted to the company's engineers and chemists for guidance and improvement. The company also has a laboratory. All members who are concerned about chemical matters may entrust the company to handle them at a low cost. (4) Any advertising and publicity matters may be entrusted to the advertising experts employed by the company to plan joint advertisements, plan exquisite advertising at low cost, and open a description of the publicity methods to notify members. Those who do not wish to join are not forced to. All procedures are handled free of charge. (5) All matters concerning trademark registration, company registration, and drafting various rules and contracts may be entrusted to the company's accountants and lawyers for handling at a low cost. (7) Group members who entrust this company to design shall follow the design service rules of Qian Yi Enterprise Silver Company. Individual members who ask this company for assistance in design research shall have the company reduce the cost of costs to encourage their research success and be hired by the company as a consultant member of the Technical Cooperation Committee. (8) If members of this association have business operations or other ongoing businesses that require financial assistance, they may entrust the company to design all ongoing plans and review the situation, or submit their existing design plans to the company for review. After the company considers the situation, it will provide appropriate financial assistance. (9) If there are any deficiencies in these articles of association, they may be amended at any time.

Since its establishment, its business has been very developed. Merchants from all over the country who are willing to promote and sign management contracts are endless. The company also cooperates with local agencies and gentry in Changzhou to promote it together. It was not long before sales reached more than 3,000 bags. The company's products are excellent, and farmers are happy to use domestic products, so this result is within expectations. It is heard that the company is now planning to organize fertilizer loan cooperatives in various provinces and counties in order to remedy the rural economy. In order to facilitate the process, it is willing to contact various agencies, groups, and schools in various places to cooperate. It is heard that the procedures are extremely simple, that is, the fertilizer produced by the company is loaned to farmers, and after the harvest is over, the farmers return the fertilizer they borrowed at a settled price. If this is done, the rural economy will be able to be remedied to a small extent. It is hoped that various agencies, group schools, and gentlemen who are interested in studying agriculture will unanimously support and cooperate together to break a bloody path in the weakening of agriculture in China, which is on the verge of collapse, and compete with imported goods.

Witness Ma Fengting Implicated in Jia Lin's Marital Dispute 166

Detained Overnight for Insulting a Public Official

Wu Bin, courtesy name Chuba, an official of the First Section of the Jiangsu Provincial Government and a native of Anhui Province, recently married a young woman named Jia Lin (号 Huixian) in the capital. Suddenly, Lin Xianjian, a native of Guangdong and the director of the Xianjian Hospital on Jiangxi Road in this city, claimed that Jia was his wife. Consequently, when Wu and Jia came to Shanghai, he accused them of bigamy. The First Special District Court issued a summons for the defendants to appear in court for interrogation. Because Jia Lin only admitted to cohabiting with Lin Xianjian, she cited Ma Fengting (also known as Ma Fengting), the doorman at No. 216 Fusheng Lane, Bazi Road, as a witness. Therefore, the court specifically issued a summons for Ma to appear in court as a witness during the second hearing. Unexpectedly, Ma was naturally crude and timid, and was unwilling to get involved in such matters that had nothing to do with him. When the time for the court hearing came, he refused to appear and spoke disrespectfully to the public official who served the summons, showing no courtesy. The public official reported the facts to the court, which then issued an arrest warrant. The day before yesterday afternoon, Ma was arrested and detained in the General Patrol Room. Yesterday morning, he was taken to the First Special Court, where Judge Qian interrogated him. According to Ma, he knew nothing about how Lin Xianjian and Jia Huixian came together. The court set the date for the continued hearing of the bigamy case as October 7th, and ordered Ma to return home, but he should surrender himself to the court for questioning when the time came. Ma's overnight detention can truly be described as being caught in the crossfire.

Bestsellers Among the Three Great Masterpieces 167

"Memoirs of a European Tour," published by the China Travel Service, is a record of Mr. Chu Minyi's travels in Europe, recalling what he saw and heard. Mr. Wu Jingheng wrote in the preface: "This is another remarkable book about human activities on Earth, a publication that can provide people with lingering memories and evoke infinite emotions, and will certainly not let Sima Qian say 'how and how'. It can beautify the past." It can be seen that the value of this book is high. Monte Carlo is the first collection of Mr. Song Chunfang's travel notes, containing twelve articles about France, Italy, Austria, Hungary, Switzerland, and China, etc. The first article is about Monte Carlo, the world's largest gambling resort in France, hence the name. The writing style is clear and elegant, forming its own unique style. "Like Passing Years" is a masterpiece by the famous novelist Mr. Zhang Henshui, describing the psychology of young people in their pursuit of education, career, and love. The deep emotions make people yearn, and the sadness makes people grieve. The structure is tortuous and unexpected, and the writing is vivid. Since the company launched the half-price joint sale of the above three books, buyers have been enthusiastic, and more than 2,000 copies have been sold. The sales locations are China Travel Service and its branches, Shanghai Bank, and major bookstores. The joint sale price is $2.15, and an additional $0.23 is charged for postage.

Table Tennis Association Launches Shanghai Open Table Tennis Competition 185

Divided into Three Groups: A, B, and C

The Shanghai Table Tennis Association recently launched a Shanghai Open Table Tennis Group Competition, divided into three groups: A, B, and C. A single round-robin cup system will be used, with the winner determined by the best of five matches. The winners of each group will then compete in a final to determine the overall champion (Shanghai Union Cup). The cup will be permanently retained by the team that wins it for three consecutive years or four times in total. Registration for membership is open from now until October 15th for the first term. Each team will pay a membership registration fee of $5, becoming a permanent member, and there will be no further fees thereafter. Each team will have seven players and three reserves. The competition will begin on October 23rd. Registration locations are as follows: Nanjing Store at the intersection of Sichuan Road and Ningbo Road; Liu Keren at the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau on Fuzhou Road; Hu Jian at the Zhonghua Jiande Association on Fusheng Road; and the Preparatory Office of the Association at No. 96 Zhongzhou Road, Zhabei. Director En of the Municipal Public Security Bureau has specially inscribed the four characters "De Xin Ying Shou" (effortlessly) as an incentive.
