Zhang Zhijiang Writes to Chu Minyi Discussing National Martial Arts Tournament Issues 189

Zhang Zhijiang, Director of the Central Guoshu Institute, replied to Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, yesterday: "I have received your letter with instructions regarding the methods for the Guoshu examination and competition. Your sincerity and enthusiasm are evident in your writing. It is a valuable text for artistic research. I have carefully read and appreciated it deeply. The fist-fighting competition in the Guoshu examination is indeed what I advocate. However, the intention behind my advocacy may not have been fully understood by you. I will explain it again. The Guoshu examination and competition are indeed aimed at encouraging excellence, but in reality, they are not limited to this. The Chinese people have been weak for years and have been oppressed by autocratic power, resulting in a near-zero level of courage. This can be seen from the collapse of the Qing army in the late Qing Dynasty without even exchanging fire with foreigners. Now, the national crisis is urgent, and the situation in the Pacific is becoming increasingly tense. In the near future, our country will definitely need a national character that can charge into battle, go through fire and water. If this is not cultivated in advance, even if we have strong ships and powerful weapons, we will inevitably be overwhelmed by fear and make mistakes, affecting the entire situation with a single move. Moreover, the world has no perfect method, and timeliness is valuable. If, today, the government encourages and rewards Guoshu competitions from above, the trend will follow, and the fields will compete to strive forward, gradually cultivating the courage to be chivalrous, brave, and unafraid in the face of the enemy. This is not without benefit to the current needs of the national crisis. This is the first point. Your letter states that in equipment competitions, each type should be carefully compared before determining the ranking. In today's situation, this is an impractical argument. In Western duels, the choice of weapons is agreed upon beforehand. However, in our country, when suddenly encountering an enemy, it is impossible to know in advance or agree upon the type of equipment. What we rely on is our skill and ability to adapt to changes. If someone who practices with a knife can only fight against a knife, and someone who practices with a sword can only fight against a sword, what happens when they suddenly meet in a narrow alley without the same equipment? Should they resist or not? The matter of martial arts is slightly different from playing chess. If someone who is good at Go meets someone who is good at Xiangqi, they simply won't place a piece, and there will be no future disaster. However, if someone using a knife refuses to fight against someone using a sword, even if I withdraw, they will stab me in the chest. What should I do? Therefore, when testing a person's skills in the examination hall, special attention should be paid to situations where the equipment is different. The examination has rules and regulations, and the competition has detailed rules. Although the equipment may be different, the principles and methods must not be disturbed. However, this year's national examination is only the second session and is still in the preliminary guidance stage. For the sake of gradual progress, there will be no competitions with different types of equipment. In the future, more advanced methods will still involve competitions with different types of equipment, hoping to achieve practical results in application. This is the second point. Furthermore, those who practice Guoshu in the world today usually only learn the forms and neglect the research of actual self-defense, competition application, and performance. The performances are diverse, but in the face of the enemy, they abandon their armor and flee. They may not like the competition method. However, they do not know that in the past, when King Xuan of Qi listened to the Yu, if they played in a group, the musicians would muddle through. But if they listened one by one, the unskilled musicians would flee. The current competition is like listening to the Yu one by one. If they only learn performance, beginners can come on stage. If they also focus on competition, those with shallow knowledge will have difficulty getting lucky.甄拔眞才誠亦莫善於此也、至於閣下盧其失手致傷、已於比賽細則中嚴加限制、重承鼎囑、自當盡力籌策、加意防護、力求周備、况數全卽漲、斷不到拚命地步、上屆業有明騐、若滬杭之役、本自標明游藝性質、似又不可與國考相提并論也、總之弟以孤陋、不敢自以爲是、仍乞卓見指敎、并允擔任評判、在事實上共同研究將來改正之點、以策進於光明、如荷惠允、何幸如之云云、

Selecting truly talented people is indeed the best way. As for accidental injuries caused by Lu Qi, strict restrictions have already been imposed in the competition rules. I reiterate my commitment to do my best to plan, protect, and strive for thoroughness. Moreover, full participation will increase the odds, and there will be no need to risk one's life. The previous session has already provided clear evidence. The battles in Shanghai and Hangzhou were explicitly marked as recreational in nature and should not be compared with the national examination. In short, with my limited knowledge, I dare not be self-righteous. I still request your insightful guidance and permission to serve as a judge, to jointly study future areas for improvement in practice, to promote progress towards enlightenment. If I am granted this, how fortunate I would be."

Diary of the British Wimbledon World Tennis Tournament (10) (1) 190

Special Correspondent from London 一志

Saturday, July 8th

Four finals were scheduled for today. By 7:30 PM, when the last mixed doubles final started on Centre Court, few spectators remained. The weather was still hot, with a hint of rain, but only a few drops fell. The first match, Mrs. Martell vs. Ms. Bride, was moved from 2:00 PM to 2:15 PM. The King and Queen of England arrived before the start of the match. Centre Court was packed, with people as numerous as grains of sand in a field.

Hopes were high beforehand that this English woman might win. However, probably none of the 15,000 spectators anticipated how close the match would be. Mrs. Martell won the first set 6-4 after each winning four games. Ms. Round won the second set 9-7. The situation after the completion of this set was, to put it mildly, pitiful and lamentable for both the players and the audience. After order was restored and the match continued, an extraordinary and unusual performance, never before seen, stunned the audience. Mrs. Martell used every kind of stroke to take the lead, winning the first set 6-3. Her foot injury was so severe that the match could barely continue in this set. At the beginning of the match, Ms. Round displayed her two fundamental strengths: first, her fluid strokes that kept the ball almost constantly in motion; second, using drop shots against Mrs. Martell, which, whether successful or not, proved to be a very effective strategy. Mrs. Martell was constantly running throughout most of the match, and towards the end, Mrs. Martell's strength to resist and defend decreased, and drop shots became less effective.

Each situation was like this: after Martell won the first set 6-4, the audience thought the second set would also be one-sided. Who knew that amazing things were just beginning? Martell served first and continued to win her serves, reaching 6-6. Both players were extremely exhausted. Ms. Round seemed to be in better spirits, and her strokes were more varied. Her forehand was powerful, her backhand reliable, and she was constantly ready to come to the net and try to put away the ball. Mrs. Martell stood at the baseline from beginning to end, hitting the ball with great care, and the placement was also very good, but with less power. Even before 6-6, her shots, and even her serves, gradually weakened. In the thirteenth game, she touched the net no less than four or five times, resulting in the failure of her serve. An unfortunate tragedy occurred in the next game. Round was down 30-40, and one of her groundstrokes landed three or four feet outside the line, but the linesman ignored it. Mrs. Martell looked at her in shock but immediately expressed her complete willingness to accept the ruling. At this time, the referee offered his opinion, saying that Mrs. Martell should win the point. It was said afterward that the referee thought the linesman had called it out. The linesman suddenly stood up from his chair and went to the referee, telling him that his ruling was irreversible. The discussion went on for some time, and the linesman on the service line also joined in. At the same time, Mrs. Martell retreated to the wooden panel behind the court, waiting with a look of panic and unease. Ms. Round was the same. It must be made clear that if Round's ball was called out, then Martell would win the game, making it 7-7. Finally, the referee declared that Round should win the point, and the score for this game became equal. Round served, and Martell made consecutive mistakes, so Round won this set 8-6.

The match never recovered from this point. Both players were in a state of panic. A drop shot from Round was not answered by Mrs. Martell. After both serving and returning, Martell only advanced a few feet inside the baseline, returning the ball very gently with a lob into Round's court. Sometimes she tried a drop shot and accidentally won. At 2-3, Round double-faulted, and the audience groaned. Martell then took a 4-2 lead but still didn't seem like a winner, as she seemed unable to move. Even balls within a few feet were abandoned. Once, she tried to answer a sideline ball, lost her footing, and fell to the ground. Then she served out again. Round then won this game. In the end, Ms. Round touched the net repeatedly, and Mrs. Martell finished 6-3. Martell's determination and ability to adapt were highly praised.

Borough's retention of the doubles championship with Buzzing was expected early on, but the process was quite laborious. In the last few games, they failed in several sets. Against Cooper and Farquharson, they were down two sets. But Borough quickly returned to his original state and regained balance, and Browning's overall performance was excellent, assisting him accordingly. Against Sato and Fujii, they lost the first set and then defeated them. In this setback, both Borough worked hard, and both sides performed brilliantly. Borough was the leader of the artillery, with balls hitting into the stands. Buzzing's defense was like a stone wall, but when necessary, he could also attack and often score points. On the other side, Sato and Fujii were more ferocious, and their ball placement was more skillful. However, their weakness was not guarding their position, which allowed the enemy to take advantage. Fujii was more active and aggressive, his shots were spectacular, but his serve was not yet satisfactory. After losing the second and third sets, this pair of Japanese players fought bravely, but ultimately could not save themselves and succumbed.

The women's doubles final was an enjoyable and interesting match. Ms. Ryan and Mrs. Matthew won. Ms. Ryan's name has appeared for the tenth time on this winner's list. Ms. James and Ms. York were completely ineffective against this fierce opponent, but in the second set, they fought hard and won 11-9. In the third set, they took a 3-1 lead, seeming hopeful. James's serve failed, and Ryan finally won the third set 6-4.

Ms. James has a talent for doubles. Her volleys and smashes were met with constant applause from the spectators. Ms. York, except for her serve, was not inferior to James in the slightest. Although she was slightly worse than her partner, she was also good at running and smashing. Both were extremely skillful, and it was a pleasure to watch. Their strategy was also similar to that of top-tier players. The main difference was that York was a natural frontcourt player, but the two exchanged positions very quickly. Ms. Ryan's shots were fierce and terrifying. Mrs. Matthew's groundstrokes from the backcourt were also powerful and fatal. Winning the mixed doubles championship at Wimbledon without losing a single set is a valuable achievement. Mrs. Cravinger and Crumb defeated Ms. Hyland and Farquharson, Mrs. Godfrey and Kingsley, Ms. Ryan and Mann, etc. The final against Hyland and Farquharson had been on the court for quite some time, a fierce battle of two sets, very long and lasting. Cravinger's stability and Crumb's versatility allowed them to return victorious. (End of full text)

The Ministry of Education Will Send a Large Number of Personnel to Inspect Local Education in Various Provinces and Cities Across the Country

To Make Preparations for Comprehensively Planning Educational Improvements Nationwide

(Nanjing, 28th) In order to understand the current state of local education in various provinces and cities across the country, the Ministry of Education will dispatch a large number of personnel, including department heads and counselors, to various provinces for on-site inspections. Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education Orders Expedited Completion of Matters That Should Have Been Handled Last Year 192

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education issued an order to the education bureaus of various counties, stating: It has been found that the 21st year of the Republic has long since ended. All educational matters promoted by the bureaus throughout the year, whether they are urgent and important, the completion of existing undertakings, the expansion of existing undertakings, or the advancement of emerging undertakings, are nothing more than administrative facilities, financial consolidation, and academic research, all of which are closely aligned with actual needs and must be implemented without delay. In order to close out the annual affairs, the department has specially conducted a review of the important matters that should have been handled by the bureaus in the 21st year. It has been found that some matters promulgated by the department have not been fully complied with, some matters approved by the counties have not yet been reported, and some matters with reporting deadlines have not been complied with at all. Such delays are highly inappropriate. Recently, it has become a common problem in administrative organs that lower levels treat orders from higher levels as mere formalities, perfunctorily fulfilling their responsibilities, and efficiency is not evident. Educational administrative organs have always valued scientific management. When implementing laws and regulations, they should be like the arm following the body's command and the finger following the arm's command, with seamless coordination from top to bottom and immediate results. It is not appropriate to feign compliance and violate orders, adopt this bad habit, or consider matters as having lost their timeliness due to inaction, and therefore shelve them. Matters that have already been handled, especially those with a continuous nature, should be inspected regularly and vigorously promoted to avoid the problem of procrastination over time. Therefore, a table of matters that must be expedited in the 21st year is specially prepared. Any bureau that has not handled or reported on a certain matter should be clearly noted in the table for easy viewing at a glance. In addition to separate orders, the aforementioned table is urgently dispatched, ordering the bureaus to conduct a review of the cases within five days of receiving the order, provide a written response on the reasons for not handling or reporting, as well as the dates for expediting the handling and reporting, and at the same time, complete and report for verification each of the items noted in the table, without further delay. This order is attached with a copy of the table of matters to be expedited in the 21st year. (Omitted)

The International Committee on Intellectual Cooperation of the International Federation of League of Nations, accepted the proposal of the Italian government to establish the International Institute for Educational Cinematography in Rome. World-Renowned Educator Dr. Suzallo Passes Away 196

Dedicated His Life to the Field of Education

A Prolific Writer

Dr. Henry Suzallo, a world-renowned educator who had previously been funded by a scholarship from steel magnate Carnegie to study education around the world, recently passed away in the hospital due to heart disease. His aspirations to develop American education also came to an end. He devoted his life entirely to the field of education. In 1915, Dr. Suzallo served as the president of the University of Washington, striving to develop the university, eventually making it one of the top universities in the country. Dr. Suzallo also served as the chairman of the Carnegie Scholarship Foundation and held supervisory positions. He traveled to Europe to study the state of education at various universities and translated the book "American Practical Education," with the aim of linking European and American education. During World War I, he served as the chairman of the Washington State Defense Bureau and a wage evaluator for the National War Labor Board. In 1918, the University of Nevada awarded him a Doctor of Laws degree, and in 1915, the University of British Columbia awarded him the same degree. He also received the title of Honorary Knight of Italy. He died at the age of 58, and people around the world mourned his loss.

Overview of Educational Administration in Fujian Province Since the Summer Vacation 197

Since Zheng Zhenwen reorganized the educational situation in Fujian Province, there has been a steady trend of progress. The various activities and facilities since the summer vacation are described below:

Military Training: The Provincial Department of Education believes that military training is extremely important during times of national crisis. It has convened military training conferences several times to discuss methods and decided that each school in the provincial capital should be divided into city and island areas. The Pacification Commissioner's Office sent personnel to coordinate the training. All students were divided into three brigades, with the first brigade divided into four companies and the second and third brigades divided into three companies. It started on July 1st and ended on July 21st, a total of three weeks. Despite the sweltering heat, the students were diligent and achieved good results.

Summer School: This year's summer school was the fifth session held. The Provincial Department of Education focused on the in-service training of primary school teachers. Therefore, the lecturers hired were all domestic primary school experts. It started on July 17th and ended on August 16th, a total of four and a half weeks of classes, with 11 subjects taught for 186 hours, 6 public lectures, 4 lectures by famous people, and 7 discussion sessions. About 300 students from various counties attended, and all were able to persevere from beginning to end. The spirit of discussion was also very sincere.

Establishment of a Science Museum: In order to meet the needs of the environment, the Provincial Department of Education decided to establish a science museum, divided into four departments: physics, chemistry, biology, and geology. Tang Shouyi, the head of the third department, and others were assigned to be responsible for the preparations. Inspector Huang Kaisheng was sent to Shanghai to purchase teaching instruments and various specimens. Currently, the purchased items have been shipped to Fujian. The official opening is scheduled for October 10th.

Statistics from the Joint Entrance Examination: (A) Participating schools and number of students: 1. 17 high schools, 241 students; 2. 87 junior high schools, 1,718 students; 3. 15 provincial primary schools, 281 students; 4. 12 normal schools, 244 students; 5. 14 vocational schools, 151 students. (B) Comparison of high school entrance examination results: 1. 3 provincial schools, 81 students, 51 graduates, 30 non-graduates; 2. 12 private schools, 160 students, 99 graduates, 61 non-graduates. (C) Comparison of junior high school entrance examination results: 1. 13 provincial schools, 348 students, 296 graduates, 79 non-graduates; 2. 21 private schools, 307 students, 193 graduates, 114 non-graduates; 3. 54 private schools, 1,076 students, 747 graduates, 279 non-graduates. (D) Comparison of subjects: Geography, Party Principles, and Biology were better in the high school group, while Mathematics, Physics, and Chemistry were worse. Geography and Party Principles were better in the junior high school group, while English and Mathematics were worse. Social Studies and Nature were better in the primary school group, while Chinese and Mathematics were the worst. (E) Comparison of schools: Provincial Polytechnic and Fuzhou High School, and Private Gezhi were better in the commercial high school group. Provincial Polytechnic, Fuzhou High School, Xiamen High School, and Private San Yi were better in the junior high school group. The county schools performed poorly, with Lianjiang, Gutian, and Fuan being the worst.

In addition, the reorganization of school staffing and the implementation of the regulations issued by the Ministry are being carried out step by step. Currently, the rampant banditry upstream has not affected the schools, and classes are still being held as usual.

Cultural Advancement in Poland 198

Recently, a Polish correspondent translated information about Polish culture, which is specially introduced below:

(1) Regarding Literature and Art: From 1928 to 1932, within five years, 176 types of Polish literary masterpieces were translated into foreign languages. Czech was the first, followed by French, and Italian ranked third. Italy has recently shown particular interest in Polish literature. Next are Russian and Ukrainian. In these two countries, works about workers' lives and social issues are prevalent. Therefore, the Polish writers admired by Soviet Russia are Strug, Sienkiewicz, Kaden-Bandrowski, and Dąbrowska. The most respected Polish literary figure abroad is Sienkiewicz, who is Poland's greatest patriotic novelist, with 53 translations. Reymont has 44 translations, Sienkiewicz 12, and Orzeszkowa 11. According to recent statistics, Polish literature ranks second only to Russian literature in terms of Slavic literature translated into foreign languages.

The wife of Foreign Minister Beck initiated a Polish literary translation exhibition in Warsaw in October. Many beautifully bound books were sent from all corners of the globe. The exhibits were extremely rich.

The Kraków literary prize decided to select the best works that have developed national culture in the past three years and award prizes to encourage them.

"Hymn of the Sea," a grand and solemn ceremony was held beside the Rosviesham lighthouse. The entire nation of Poland paid tribute to renowned writer and poet Jan Kasprowicz, who praised the sea. Minister Szawarski gave a speech on behalf of the government, and after other speeches, he proposed renaming a navigational lighthouse the Jan Kasprowicz Lighthouse and erecting a temporary memorial plaque. General 理其椎塞 specially stated that the entire nation of Poland has a deep love for the sea, as Poland's outlet to the sea is related to the security of national defense. An international photo exhibition was held in Kraków last month with over 5,000 works. The United States and the Czech Republic had the most. An international woodcut exhibition was held in Warsaw this month, which attracted great attention abroad. England, France, Germany, the United States, Austria, Belgium, Canada, Spain, the Czech Republic, the Netherlands, Italy, Switzerland, Hungary, Sweden, Latvia, Romania, Bulgaria, and Japan all sent exhibits.

It was decided in November of this year to open a Polish art exhibition in Soviet Russia. The Polish government has appointed Janowski, the director of the Kraków Academy of Fine Arts, as a special commissioner to prepare for the exhibition and liaise with the Soviet Russian government in Moscow.

The Polish government has participated in the International Religious Art Exhibition held in Rome, displaying photos and charts of modern religious architectural trends. In addition to the government, Polish artists have also participated in a personal capacity.

A bust of Mussolini was sculpted by a Polish female sculptor, Mrs. Stelelicka, and is nearing completion. The Italian Prime Minister has posed for it several times. Mrs. Stelelicka has also created portraits of Princess Deby Mont and the Crown Prince's wife. This portrait of Mussolini will be placed on the航輪 "Ocean." This work has received very good reviews.

The 250th anniversary of the Polish King Sobieski III's defeat of Turkey in Vienna and the 70th anniversary of the 1863 anti-Russian revolution were commemorated by collecting designs to create new coins. The Postal and Telegraph Department also issued new commemorative stamps.

(2) Regarding Music: The opera "Halka" by the 19th-century Polish composer is gradually gaining attention from the foreign art scene. It will be performed at the National Opera House in Bern, the capital of Switzerland, and Belgrade, the capital of Yugoslavia, this autumn.

The modern young composer Machiniuski is highly praised by the Polish literary, artistic, and educational circles. Renowned Polish piano virtuoso Rubinstein has adopted Mach's compositions for regular performances. Mach has recently traveled abroad to increase his recognition among foreign audiences.

The "Sea Publicity Day" committee openly solicited a score entitled "Poland's Eulogy to the Sea." Rowviski won the first prize. Poland's respect for the sea can be said to be meticulous.

Professor Moross has been selected by the Scientific and Artistic Council of the Warsaw Conservatory of Music as the president of the conservatory from 1933 to 1936.

The Warsaw National Academy of Dramatic Art has decided to establish a scenery school in the near future, with the famous playwright and director 列氏 as the director of scenery. Establishing a specialized school to study and train specialized talents is still a pioneering effort in Europe.

The International Conference on the History of Art was held in Stockholm, the capital of Sweden, in September this year. Representatives from 25 countries participated. More than ten Polish scholars went to attend and give lectures.

(3) Regarding Science: The International Historical Conference was held in Warsaw at the end of August. There were more than 500 foreign representatives participating, including 140 from universities and other scientific institutions. There were more than 400 papers. The scope of the conference was divided into 15 parts, such as the organization of historical research, archaeology, prehistoric events, ancient, medieval, and modern history, religious history, legal history, economic history, cultural history, art history, the history of science, literary history, and historical theories. After the conference, a travel itinerary was prepared, and many world historical authorities attended.

Astronomer 克敏斯基, the director of the Warsaw Observatory, has been studying the 無爾狐 star for 20 years. He recently published his theory on the movement of this star, which has been recognized by the Royal Astronomical Society of England, which made him a member. In addition, 克氏's calculations have been verified by the California Observatory in the United States for their accuracy. (4) Regarding Film: The exchange of newsreel films has been contracted by the Polish Telegraph Agency's film department with foreign countries. The company is the main producer of Polish newsreel films. It has signed exchange agreements with nine countries, including France, Italy, Switzerland, Hungary, Yugoslavia, Belgium, Spain, and the Czech Republic, exchanging one foot for one foot, and transporting at least 200 meters of film to major contract countries each month.

The Central Film Bureau recently released the 1932 cinema statistics, totaling 752 cinemas with 256,871 seats. In Warsaw, the capital of Poland, there are 54 cinemas, 51 of which are equipped with sound film facilities, and only three specialize in silent films.

In addition, 波人 謝星斯基 presented a plan to the International Institute for Educational Cinematography in Rome, suggesting that film is the best method for scientific research and technical inventions, which has attracted the attention of the association.

Belgium has recently screened eight Polish films. The Brussels Evening Post printed a photo of the female star 石英沙爾斯基 and praised her incessantly.

The Municipal Education Association Rectifies People's Schools 200

The Shanghai Municipal Education Association yesterday issued an order to the people's schools, stating: This association has been running people's schools for several months, and various regulations have been formulated and issued one after another, ordering compliance. Vocational Education Society to Hold Vocational Guidance Symposium Today 203

The China Vocational Education Society, in response to the Ministry of Education's promulgation of measures for vocational guidance in secondary schools, believes it is urgent to convene authorities from various schools to conduct research to promote its effective implementation. (2) That all schools should regularly lead senior students to visit agricultural, industrial, and commercial institutions to increase their practical knowledge and foster social experience. (3) That all schools establish a student personality, academic ability, talent, and interest survey to be sent to the institutions of higher learning or employment that the students attend after graduation.

Spring and Autumn

Autumn's Combinations 204

— Zhan Lu

No wonder the world laments autumn. Just look, the combinations that form the word "autumn" never have a good meaning. The old sage Cangjie already laid out the feng shui, so what's there to say!

If you don't believe me, let me give a few examples: Autumn on the heart is the "sorrowful" *chou*; autumn on the bird is the "oriole" *ying*, as in "the balding oriole cries" in history; the oriole is not a good bird. Autumn by the side of a person is the "ignore" *chou*, as in the *Romance of the Western Chamber*: "If he doesn't *chou* (acknowledge) people, what can one do?" *Chou* is not a welcome treatment. *Chou* is not a welcome treatment. Autumn by the side of the eye is the "glare" *chou* of "give him a *chou* (glare)"; *chou* is not a good look; autumn by the side of the hand is a "seize" *jiu*, like one grabs with their hand, autumn is not a good gesture; autumn by the side of metal is the "shovel" *qiao* used by corrupt officials to dig up the land, *qiao* is not a good tool; autumn by the side of the mouth is the "chirp" *jiu* of "the sky is gloomy and the ghosts cry *jiu jiu*," *jiu* is not a good sound; autumn by the side of water is the "narrow" *qiu* of a *qiu* place, *qiu* is not a good place. Autumn by the side of fish is a *qiao* (mud loach) in the mud, *qiao* is not a good fish. In conclusion, no matter how you combine it, you cannot find a word formed with the character "autumn" that is grand, rich, happy, or comfortable. No matter how you wear out every kind of dictionary, new or old, is there one? No, simply none.

If we were to say the line, "Another year has easily passed with the autumn wind," the seven characters already contain a kind of desolation. Change it to the word "spring," and "Another year has easily passed with the spring breeze," then there is the hope of "ten thousand things returning to spring," and one doesn't feel desolate at all. Therefore, national events don't necessarily happen in autumn; however, people always say, "the autumn of many events." National difficulties also don't necessarily happen in autumn; however, people always say, "the autumn of many difficulties." Try looking through various idioms to find a phrase "the summer of many difficulties" or "the summer of many events." Is there one? No, simply none!

Looking at it factually, national humiliation commemorations mostly occur in May, clearly the summer of many difficulties and the summer of many events; but with the extraordinary humiliation of September 18th, "the autumn of many events" and "the autumn of many difficulties" actually transformed from idioms into reality. How unfortunate is that!

The commemoration of September 18th has already passed ten days, but please, people, do not forget the autumn of many events and the autumn of many difficulties.

The Gaochang Deity 205

— Fu Yizhi

Is this probably the Gaochang Deity on patrol?

Silence, make way! Banners reading "Silence," "Clear the Way," "Censorate," "Marquis of Yongning," "Gaochang Deity," etc., were carried on the shoulders of men in red, crossing the main road in a V-formation. Following them were fellow countrymen wearing embroidered silk sashes, high red hats, and each holding a square flag inlaid with the characters "Kitchen Quick." Behind them came two rows of gentlemen with red-topped hats and white silk shirts, Qiaoqi gauze jackets, holding copper incense burners. After that came the ten-section gong and drum team. Bringing up the rear, I heard, was the Gaochang Deity. These fellow countrymen walking in front of the Gaochang Deity must be the Deity's subordinates and guards making their appearance?

"The Master is coming, stop and clear the way!"

The Gaochang Deity, wearing a tall crown and court robes, sat in a frame carried by four people, looking quite majestic! Just as the divine palanquin was about to cross the road, a truck drove up from the left, and a tram filled with passengers came from the right. His incense-bearing disciples, fearing they would offend the divine might, shouted frantically, and the tram and the truck finally stopped.

Who exactly was the former incarnation of the Gaochang Deity? I am not a historian and have not consulted the Shanghai County Records (perhaps these records can be consulted). Offering a brick to attract jade, I can only await the clear instruction of researchers. But because the Gaochang Deity so pompously paraded through the streets, I couldn't help but think of two hapless deities in Jiangxi:

One is the famous alchemist and author of *Baopuzi* from the Jin dynasty, Ge Hong. On Mount Ge Xian (named after him) in Qianshan County, Jiangxi, there is a magnificent temple dedicated to him. Every year in August, people from seven or eight nearby counties come to the mountain to burn incense, numbering no less than tens of thousands. It is said that incense pilgrims who were not ritually clean would be punished by him until they were half-dead. However, recently, his temple was burned to the ground by so-called "rebels." The other is Li Deyu, who entered the position of Chancellor during the reign of Emperor Wu of Tang. He ascended to immortality on Mount Ling in Shangrao. Each year, people came to worship him in no fewer numbers than Ge Hong, and in years of drought, receiving this Old Immortal Li (his immortal title) was essential for rain. It is said that his temple was also burned down by the Communists the year before last.

Similarly, one is an immortal deity, but because they are located in different places, their experiences differ. Could it be that gods also have good and bad luck? The worthlessness of idol worship should be clear from this. Why are the civilized people of Shanghai so deluded?

Watching Dancing at a Dance Hall 206

— Wang Yingyue

On Saturday night, Miss Li, a "butterflies" (socialite) friend, took me to the dance hall where she goes every night to have fun. Although my heart trembled with a bit of inferiority and hesitation, my legs seemed eager to explore, and I followed her to our destination.

The surroundings of the dance hall were very quiet, without any of the noisy city air. Colored glass tubes reflected from the yellow mud-like short walls, tinting my white shirt a light purple. Across the street, there were a dozen newly painted cars parked. At the entrance, some small boys in copper buttoned white canvas uniforms and a security guard were joking.

Stepping through the gate, there was a garden with green grass and trees, and the scenery was particularly pleasant under the cloak of night. From the entrance, a path led directly to the dance hall, and the surroundings of the dance hall were all made of agate, crystal clear, which made people reluctant to leave.

Inside the dance hall sat many beautiful girls, curly hair, black eyebrows, red lips, high breasts, jade-colored arms, soft legs, filled the air with temptation, seven or eight youths with numb nerves, their dark eyes searching like sea-exploring lights.

The melodious music began, and the whole hall was filled only with a lush, intoxicating green light. The men and women also left their seats one after another, he and she, she and she, pairs of them embracing tightly, rotating back and forth in the middle according to the rhythm of the music! Rotating! Rotating!

Their spirits were indeed a little excited, but this excitement contained a deep sense of boredom! Time flew by moment by moment, and they kept embracing each other again and again, like puppets without any human emotion.

"A paradise on earth!" Feeling a little tired, I escaped from this enjoyment den of gigolos like Algiers, sighing softly.

The cool breeze of nature swept away the artificial scent I had picked up, and it was already eleven o'clock when I walked home alone.

The Northeast Fourth Company Commander 207

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Sixteen: Bitter Feelings Still Bring Blessings, Hurried Military Affairs Secretly Shift the Troops

Gui Zhi told me that for the sake of her livelihood, she dared not offend her brother, believing me to be a money-grabbing person. But as for herself, she could abandon a friend in need and marry the current company commander. A company commander is just a junior officer at best, so what's so great about that? Thinking of this, she couldn't help but clench her fist and slam it on the table. The waiter was carrying a cup of coffee in both hands, about to place it on the table, when he heard the thud, splashing the water in the cup all over the saucer. He shrank back and stared blankly at Ji Zhi. Ji Zhi herself immediately realized what had happened. She smiled and said, "You haven't been open for a year, so why is this table so unsteady?" The waiter then realized that she was actually adjusting the table for him, and he had misunderstood. So, with a smile, he placed the coffee cup on the table, but his eyes still kept glancing at her. Ji Zhi saw that the sugar cube jar was in the middle of the table, so she used the copper tongs to put a sugar cube in the cup, and then another sugar cube, her eyes shooting beyond the sugar jar. Her whole body was numb, not knowing what she was doing. Suddenly, she looked down and saw that the sugar cubes in the coffee cup were already sticking out of the water. How sweet should the coffee be with all this sugar in it? So, seeing that no one was around, she picked the sugar cubes out of the cup. Her original intention was to take them out and put them in the saucer under the cup. But her eyes were fixed on a snack price list on the opposite wall. By the time she finished reading the price list, things were even worse. She had scooped up all the sugary water, including the sediment, into a plate of egg cakes. This was really terrible. If the waiter saw it, wouldn't he think she had gone crazy? She turned around and saw that the waiter wasn't there. Then, unexpectedly, she dumped the plate of egg cakes into the spittoon. As soon as she finished dumping, the waiter came. (200)

Shattered Youth 208

— Ziwei

A delicate and beautiful flower, when it is budding and in full bloom, fragrant and rich, is most likely to attract the attention of wandering butterflies and bees. But, unable to withstand the rain and wind, the flower will wither and fall. At this time, the bees and butterflies have already flown to other branches and will no longer come to pay their respects or feel sorry.

A beautiful and good woman, in the prime of her youth, is just like a fresh flower. But her pure will, unable to withstand the pursuit of the opposite sex and the temptation of vanity, is most likely to go astray. Once her beauty fades and her reputation is tarnished, it is like a flower that has gone through wind and rain, and the past is like a dream, unbearable to look back on!

Today's modern women, before tasting that kind of bitterness, are reveling in revelry with the opposite sex, like being drunk, talking about love, and enjoying the scenery to the fullest. How do they know that good dreams don't last long? When the other party's purpose is achieved, they are abandoned like leftovers and not worth a second glance. At this time, even if she is sad and painful, it is too late to regret.

The new film "Remnant Spring" by the Star Film Company, which will be released at the New Light Theater on October 1st, can be used as a mirror for today's modern women. Jin Meili (played by Ms. Xu Lai, the standard beauty of the East) in the play is a completely modern girl, but her result is taking poison and sacrificing herself.

Modern girls must remember that youth is the easiest to waste. Quickly turn the time spent on enjoyment and talking about love to striving for social causes! Wasting youth will only make you like fallen flowers and flowing water, unrecoverable. Jin Meili in "Remnant Spring" is the best lesson.

Correction: In the previously published article by Mr. Tu Jiangxia, "China is Full of Gold," it was stated that the Italian priest Matteo Ricci came to China to preach and wrote "Oriental Journey" after returning to his country. Ricci was actually a mistake for Polo. Yesterday, Mr. Zhan Ru of Jiangwan explained everything in detail. This is to correct the error and thank Mr. Zhan Ru.

Prelude

General Mobilization of Laughter 209

— Yu

A smile, less a sorrow; laughter is something that stimulates the appetite and is good for the spirit, beneficial to people. However, inducing laughter is also a difficult thing. First, the vulgar and rude words like those in the bars, and the general inappropriateness like a bedpan as a hat or a pot (pottery) of wine in shadow plays, are not for the upper class. Then there's another kind, where you think it's extremely funny, but before the words are even out of your mouth, you burst into loud laughter yourself. In this breathless narration, no matter how well you speak, it will only make people listen with a forced smile, putting on a Laurel-like awkward face. Therefore, to induce laughter, the first thing is to have a Buster Keaton-like deadpan face, and then, with that deadpan face, tell a joke.

The Turtle Who Studied the *Romance of the Three Kingdoms* Thoroughly

At a banquet, a friend who liked to talk a lot was telling wild stories. He told a story about a storyteller who ridiculed a storyteller who told longer stories. On the day of the birthday of Zhang Tianjun, the Great Emperor of the North Pole, he ordered his turtle and snake generals to say that any immortals who came to offer birthday wishes and violated the precepts of wine, lust, wealth, and anger would be turned away. The two generals obeyed the Great Emperor's command and guarded the mountain gate. Before long, an immortal came riding on a cloud. The snake general, seeing that it was Lü Dongbin, hurried forward to stop him and recited the Heavenly Decree. Lü Xian asked how he had violated the four precepts. The snake general replied, "You were drunk three times in Yueyang Tower, violating the wine precept; you teased Bai Mudan three times, violating the lust precept; you turned stones into gold and cut down the Yellow Dragon with your sword, violating the wealth and anger precepts. You have violated all four precepts, how can you offer birthday wishes?" Lü Xian, hearing this, left indignantly. After a while, Guan Yu came riding on Red Hare, holding his Green Dragon Crescent Blade. The turtle general, seeing this, hurried forward to stop him and recited the Great Emperor's edict to Guan Yu. Guan Yu, hearing this, stroked his long beard and asked the turtle general to state the precepts he had violated. The turtle general also spoke eloquently, "A large banquet every ten days, a small banquet every five days, violating the wine precept; a tael of gold to mount the horse, a tael of silver to dismount, violating the wealth precept; slaying Diaochan under the moon, slaying six generals at five passes, violating the wealth and lust precepts." Guan Gong, not waiting for him to finish, raised his silkworm eyebrows, widened his phoenix eyes, held his big knife, and shouted angrily, "You turtle, you speak the *Romance of the Three Kingdoms* so thoroughly!" When Mr. So-and-so said this, he even acted out the gestures, quite pleased with himself. A humorist, hearing this, suddenly asked Mr. So-and-so to repeat Guan Yu's words. Mr. So-and-so said loudly again, "You turtle, you speak the *Romance of the Three Kingdoms* so thoroughly!" But the sound of laughter suddenly erupted from the whole gathering, but Mr. So-and-so was still complacent.

Well-Field System and Warfare 210

A certain teacher, while lecturing on history, when discussing the well-field system, said eloquently that the well-field system was to dig a well in the center of each field, so that in drought years, water could be drawn from the well to irrigate the fields, so as not to be like digging a well when one is thirsty, impossible to salvage. A certain student, hearing this, stood up and said, "According to what the teacher said, if the well-field is explained this way, then the two words 'warfare' in the book must mean that each soldier eats a knife, and if the soldiers are all killed, no wonder the world will be in great chaos." The professor, hearing this, was stunned and did not know how to answer.

How Would They Know I Am a Patriotic Youth? 211

There was a patriotic youth in Suzhou who, after the January 28th Truce Agreement, had resolved to go north and go beyond the borders to resist Japan. At the same time, he sent out many letters to inform his friends of his determination to resist Japan. But several days after the farewell banquet, he was still lingering with his sisters and had not yet set off. So, a group of friends who had given him the farewell banquet asked him when he would depart. The youth, hearing this, said with a look of grief and trepidation, "I have been preparing to leave for a long time, but I can't bear to leave the women here." The friends, hearing this, all said, "Aren't there women over there too? You can go after them as much as you like!" The youth's attitude became even more distressed, and he said sadly, "But how would the women over there know that I am a patriotic youth!"

A Cigarette Factory Opened in His Pocket 212

A stingy friend, his cigarettes mostly came from friends, never buying them with his own money. One day, he bummed another cigarette from a friend. After taking a few puffs, he couldn't smoke anymore because he had other things to do. But how could he willingly sacrifice that long cigarette butt? So, he put out the fire on the edge of the table and hid it in the inner pocket of his clothes where he always stored cigarettes. Who knew that the embers of the cigarette butt were not completely extinguished and actually caught fire again, and the two cigarette butts already in his pocket, along with it, emitted wisps of white smoke. By the time that friend realized it, sparks were already flying straight up, and it was impossible to salvage. After finally putting it out, his pocket was already burned through and his clothes were torn. A joker, seeing his comical face, teased him, "A cigarette factory has opened in your pocket, so you don't have to ask people for cigarettes anymore!" Amidst the laughter of others, that friend's face became even more comical.

Sunny Weather Turns Cotton Prices Softer 221

Influx of New Grain, Rice Prices Plunge 223

South Shanghai: Yesterday, after a long period of rain, the weather cleared and nearly 60 boats arrived in succession, further softening confidence. Local store customers were also watching before the festival, and sales were particularly sluggish for out-of-town buyers. Prices for all goods plunged, with new goods, which accounted for two-thirds of the arrivals, being particularly affected. Changbang, Su Tongbang, and broke-grain Chenjian rice fell by 0.2 yuan. Nanhang thick rice, due to the large number of arrivals, was discounted by about 0.4 yuan. Qingjiao, Song Si thin rice, and new tip rice prices were more active, and the market was slightly tighter, with 1,300-1,400 bags traded. Prices were reduced by 0.1 yuan. The rest of the new rice prices fell by 0.3-0.4 yuan. Yin Yuan goods were scarce and remained stable. Yuan rice was still unavailable.

North Shanghai: Over 50 boats arrived from various regions, and sales of all goods were sluggish. Broken grain, Dingxi new grain, thin rice, Xinbu Dujian, prices down slightly by 0.1 yuan. Medium grade Xi Xin Geng, Dong Xin Geng, Ling Bai Jian, Tuan Jian, prices reduced by 0.1-0.2 yuan. New and old Yang Jian, Chen Dujian, Bai Yuan and other prices fluctuated slightly.

Ke Hsien Rice Arrivals Gradually Increase 224

Ke Hsien rice saw a surge in arrivals yesterday. The market price had soared by 0.5-0.6 yuan a week prior, and prices had been rising steadily until the day before yesterday, when they began to return to normal. During this upward period, traders were quite active. Goods from Nanjing and its vicinity had been arriving repeatedly, and Shanghai warehouses had stores. As for Hunan goods, which require a six-to-seven-day journey, shipments only began arriving in port the day before yesterday. Yesterday, 16,500 bags of new rice arrived, and samples were already being sent out. The Minbang (Fujian) were the most eager buyers, and the Ao Province (Macau) and Shantou were more active. The provincial capital gang in Shantou had sent people to Changsha to contact the joint government-merchant production and sales committee in that area, seeking direct transport to reduce intermediate losses. The Chaozhou gang focused on Wuhu rice, which they had been purchasing in Wuhu for years, and were particularly eager to buy recently. Therefore, sales in Shanghai did not see activity from the Guangzhou and Chaozhou gangs. The Shantou gang focused on applying for loading in Shanghai, and were interested in Xiang rice and Jing rice. Yesterday, they applied to load 1,985 bags of Xiang Province coarse rice at prices of 5.9-5.5 yuan, and 1,500 bags of Jingji Hsien rice at prices of 7-6.5 yuan. 187 bags of Jiangxi late Ji were purchased by the gang at a price of 7.85 yuan. Also, 700 bags of Yang Jian were priced at 7.6-7.45 yuan. The arrival of rice was strong yesterday, and the price of each grade fell by a few cents.

Silk and Tea: High-Grade Zhuang Zhenmei Tea Sells Well at Firm Prices 229

Wuyuan Zhuang standard Zhenmei was quoted at one hundred and thirty-five yuan. Market prices were quite firm. However, high-grade Zhuang teas were exceptionally scarce in the market, and low-grade teas often did not meet sales expectations, resulting in sluggish trading. Similarly, Gongxi Needle-like teas also mirrored the Zhenmei tea situation, showing a trend of rising high-grade and suppressing low-grade teas.

Oil Market: Soybean Oil Suffers a Sharp Decline After a Half-Month of Resistance 230

The soybean oil market suffered from a decline in buying power due to continuous telegrams and lower production prices. Efforts to resist this decline have lasted for half a month. However, selling pressure is now unavoidable. As a result, yesterday, the market opened prices for various soybean oils, but there were significant differences compared to prices from two weeks prior. Ship-borne Dalian oil prices were only reduced by forty-five cents due to limited supply. Ship-borne Qishan oil fell by seventy cents, while Niuzhuang oil stocks surged, resulting in a sharp decline. Ship-borne cargo fell by eighty cents, and wheel-transported cargo fell by ninety cents. (See the market price column for prices and transaction volumes.)

Free Talk

"Eating Religion" 231

— Yu Fengzhi

Mr. Da Yi, in "The Dream of Literary Domination," criticizes Liu Xie for "shaming the sages" because Liu Xie claimed to have begun writing after dreaming of Confucius, but later became a monk. In fact, since the Northern and Southern Dynasties, Chinese literati and scholars, Daoists and monks, have generally been characterized by a "lack of special dedication." Famous figures since the Jin Dynasty each had three little hobbies: first, the "Analects" and the "Classic of Filial Piety"; second, "Laozi"; and third, the "Vimalakirti Sutra." They not only used these as talking points but also often wrote commentaries. During the Tang Dynasty, there were debates between the three religions, which later turned into everyone mocking each other. It was not a big deal for so-called famous Confucians to write a few inscriptions for Buddhist temples. Song Dynasty Confucians looked solemn but secretly appropriated Chan Buddhist sayings. In the Qing Dynasty, not long ago, we still knew that Confucian scholars believed in the "Book of Great Inducement" and the "Yin Zhi Wen of Emperor Wenchang," and would even invite monks to their homes to perform repentance rituals.

When Christianity was introduced to China, Christians considered themselves believers, but ordinary people outside the religion called them "eaters of religion." These two words truly captured the "spirit" of the believers, and could also encompass most believers in Confucianism, Buddhism, and Daoism, as well as be applied to many old heroes who "eat the revolutionary rice."

People in the Qing Dynasty called the eight-legged essay a "knocking brick," because once you obtained fame and status, it was like opening a door, and the brick was no longer needed. In recent years, there have been so-called arguments in magazines. The emergence of "XX Review" was not due to oppression but because the authors of this group were soaring. The decline of "New Moon" was because the old members had all "climbed" up, and were far away from the moon. To distinguish this kind of thing from the "knocking brick," we should call it a "ladder to heaven."

"Religion" in China has always been like this. Talking about revolution is one thing; talking about loyalty and filial piety is another; circling with the Grand Lama is another; building pagodas and hiding doctrines is another. In an era suitable for exclusive "eating," the focus should be on one supreme authority. In an era suitable for "eating" together, the various religions are not fundamentally different, except that one dish is a whole duck, and the other is a mixed assortment. Liu Xie was the same, merely changing from "not sprinkling ginger" to eating vegetarian food. There was no difference in the amount in the stomach. Moreover, for a monk to annotate the "Analects," the "Classic of Filial Piety," or "Laozi" is still a kind of "heavenly principle," isn't it?

The Beginning of Opium Import into China 232

— Zi Zhan

In my "Qulu's Mutterings" article on the people of Sichuan and opium, I cited the poem of Yong Tao, a Shu person of the late Tang Dynasty, as evidence, stating that opium already existed in China as early as the Li Tang Dynasty. Recently, in the twelfth volume, eighth book of the Complete Tang Poems, I saw Li Zhenbai's poem praising poppy seeds:

Inverted arrangement of Shuanglu pieces, sparsely inserted jasper ivory counters.

Resembles both sacrificial cow milk and a bag of jingling horse bells.

Drumsticks and waterfall arrows have their origin.

I say that the Chinese already grew opium in the Tang Dynasty, this is also evidence. Wu Yu's "History of the Opium War" says that the Sino-foreign opium trade had been going on for many years before the Opium War. It states that poppy seeds were imported by Arab merchants as early as the Zhenyuan period of the Tang Dynasty. Xiao Yishan's "Comprehensive History of the Qing Dynasty" and Chen Huai's "Outline of Qing History" hold the same view, but I do not know on what basis. The "Old Book of Tang, Biography of the Western Regions" states that the country of Fulin sent envoys in the second year of Qianfeng to present "diyejia," and some suspect that "diyejia" is the poppy, but it is also unknown whether this is true. The Qing Confucian Yu Zhengxie's "Gui Yi Lei Gao" quotes the Tang translation of the "Vinaya Miscellaneous Matters Sutra," stating that the sick inhale smoke through two bowls joined together with a hole in the bottom, fire in the middle to burn the medicine, and a twelve-finger-long iron pipe placed in the hole to inhale it. However, it is not known whether Indian opium entered China together with the Buddhist scriptures at that time. The opium that first anesthetized our spiritual values then that same opium anesthetized the flesh. The red-headed ××'s poison is in China; how could it merely be foreign port big capitalists, those who work with the tiger, be accomplices!

Reading "Diary of a Madman" 233

— Zhou Lengjia

While sorting through old books, I accidentally came across a copy of "A Call to Arms" that I bought eight years ago.

The blood-red cover, although somewhat dimmed, its spirit seems indestructible. Opening it, each and every word is still like being carved on wood.

The nostalgia was awakened. Unconsciously, I picked up the book and continued reading. I wanted to see if the current era has some similarities with the era depicted in the book. In other words, whether the environment in "A Call to Arms" has passed.

The first piece is "Diary of a Madman."

The madman in "Diary of a Madman" suspects that everyone around him wants to eat him, and he draws various pieces of evidence from all directions to prove that they are all cannibals. He cannot even feel safe with the dog of the Zhao family giving him a glance. Eight years ago, when I first read this piece, I only found the madman in the book ridiculously and pitifully neurotic. But now, I cannot laugh. I can only fix my serious gaze on the book.

Undoubtedly, the era has dragged me into the book, making me similar to the madman in "Diary of a Madman." I still remember very clearly how the era persecuted me the year after "A Call to Arms" came into my hands. Around me, whether in my family or in society, everywhere was filled with people who wanted to eat me, with eyes that wanted to eat me. At that time, I also burned my beloved books with tears in my eyes, and I also fled outside and lived a life of exile with tears in my eyes. I was really afraid even when a dog glanced at me. Luckily, my birth chart was good, and I was able to leak out from the teeth of these cannibals. But looking back at other young people who "were born at the wrong time" and were eaten by cannibals, not even leaving their bones behind, I cannot help but be frightened and gasp.

Even now, although I am living a different kind of life, I still feel surrounded by cannibals. Occasionally going out, getting on a tram or a bus, I carefully look around, and everyone has a fierce look on their faces, staring intently, as if they cannot wait to swallow me whole, causing my heart to beat wildly.

Even in the literary world that I respect, it now seems that a corner has been occupied by cannibals. Some of them will openly sell their friends, some will fabricate rumors under pseudonyms, and insidiously slander, all wanting to eat the flesh and blood of others to expand their own Western-style houses. This makes me, who had the ambition to be a small soldier in the cultural movement eight years ago, shrink back.

"When will the era of 'Diary of a Madman' finally pass?" Looking at the gloomy sky outside the window, I cannot help but sigh.

Travel Notes 234

— Tianma

5. Jiang Recievers and Callers

In this trip, two kinds of people are most admired and fearful of me, that is Jiang Receivers and Callers. For these two kinds of people, consistently, I abide by the lessons of the second gentleman Confucius to respect the gods and stay away from them.

"Jiang Recievers" are hotel's special envoy to the ship to pick up guests-no, solicit business, and callers, everyone knows that is the peddler selling snacks or local specialties. These two kinds of people have the diplomat-like words, warrior-like courage, fox-like cunning, monkey-like agility, and also like brown sugar with a soft劲, no matter who, as long as they are valued, they will spend a lot of effort to get rid of.

Whenever the ship is approaching the pier, far away, you can see the group of heroes, like preparing for a hundred-yard race, everyone energetic waiting on the pier. As soon as the ship docks, a shout and the soldiers rushed to the front of the enemy, desperately squeezed on the ship, desperately run up. That situation is really like "mercury leaks into the ground, not permeable. Then it is "Fortune Hotel", "Yangtze River Restaurant", "Eggs", "New peanuts," trying to scream as if deliberately competing for who has the loudest voice, who is strong enough, so the ship will immediately be crowded and noisy into a mess.

If at this time your door is not closed, and you also want to see the comedy outside the door, immediately, the heroes will come to you, first a kindly smiling face, and then softly said: "Sir, are you here again? Still live with us, OK? Prices are fair, hospitality is thoughtful, sir is also an old customer,..." This will really make you flattered, and can not answer. Whether you have been to this port, he always asserts that you are their old customer, whether you go ashore, he always advises you to fall into their inn, so, easily, one goes, and one comes, the words are this set, and people do their best. At this time, although you will feel trouble, but you will never sincerely admire their talent.

After Jiang Reciever leaves, the caller will then come, also first a smiling face, then sing all his goods' nicknames, and then take one by one to your eyes. For example, it is selling Wuhu dried bean curd, he will say: "Look, this dried curd is so good. Also fragrant, also tender, take some back, both good for yourself to eat, but also good for sending people, on the turn Sir not bought a hundred or two? Old customer, this time buy some more!" By analogy to sell Nanjing salted duck or sell Jiujiang porcelain, the words are always this set, especially everyone will definitely recognize that you are his old customer, last time you bought a lot, this time there is a re-buy "obligation". So, also one left, another came, no matter you shake your head, you refuse out loud, even scold him to get out, he is still that kind and good-natured, still that kind of sincerely advise you, until you accept his advice, or you slap the door shut with force.

For these two heroes, I never dared to ask for advice, the ship was about to approach the pier, I had already closed the door, only dared to peek in the window, so the heroes also seem to have "hope and not be able to reach" indignation!

I thought, when the September 18th Incident broke out the year before last, if we had sent these two kinds of talents to Geneva to appeal for rescue, the great powers would probably not have stood by as they do today!

In a Third-Class Carriage (Continued) 235

— Ba Jin

The train left Pukou in the drizzling rain. It was eleven o'clock. I did not leave my footprints in Nanjing, and I regret it. I have several friends in Nanjing. I should have gone to see them. I should have set aside some time to spend with them, but the rain stopped me. What I especially miss is that friend who is suffering from a disease and his wife. He recently wrote to me saying: "Your pure and great spirit, your unrestrained and relaxed life, whenever I have a moment of calmness, I think of you: I am gradually buried deeper and deeper and become a mud man. I often hope to end my life early because I have a chronic illness." Last year, in Beiping, I received his hospitality for more than a week. I spent those nights with him in the same bed, listened to his coughs and mutterings many times. I left a pair of stone balls that I bought in the Summer Palace in that small apartment and left. The impression he left on me has not faded to this day, it is still as vivid as last year: pure and great spirit, only he can receive this evaluation. But no one has ever understood him. Now he is weakening day by day in the struggle of a difficult life, under the contemptuous eyes of society. Every time I read his prose mixed with blood and tears, my whole soul is disturbed. I often shout madly in my heart: He cannot die, he should live on, become strong, and enjoy the happiness in life.

My thoughts turned like wheels. But the rain gradually lessened. At one stop, the rain stopped completely. The weather was still bad. The pressure on my heart has not eased either. But the train is moving forward again, like a roaring, hungry beast.

There were not many passengers in the carriage. Many seats were empty. One person could occupy a chair. The carriage was new. The color of the paint was bright, and it was washed very clean. There were blinds. These made an old guest on the opposite side exclaim in surprise from time to time.

The weather later improved. The sun peeked out from the clouds. Outside the train window were trees, fields, and mountains, but I remembered every moment that I was going north.

Passionate Children (2) 236

— Translated by Ge Mang and Sai Zuoying

And this crisp, beautiful sound, even when saying the most trivial things, contains a kind of flattery: "Godfather, would you like to move your chair to the porch?" She talks about Paris, she talks about the exhibition and the white palaces towering on the banks of the Seine. If you can go to this place to play, it must be very happy thing, so he dreams of that magnificent and incredible magical city. He hopes to go there with her.

"But if this makes you happy, good boy, you come after lunch on Sunday. White Duck only has four days to play with us; we can take a car to the green forest for a ride."

× × × × ×

Roger's thoughts became unusually uneasy. He did not even like to eat, and his grandmother blamed him for being angry with his belly, blaming him for being emotional. He was not hungry, but he had no pain; a hidden cold and heat in the body was raising him. He anxiously waited for Sunday to come. He ran to the Parc de Saint-Cloud filled with the fragrance of roses to dream. He made up some very gentle songs, as if this music was coming from his heart. He made many verses that he felt were so beautiful that they brought tears to his eyes:

The sky is like blue satin,

May filled with the fragrance of wild roses

Pours some pearls in the jewelry box!

In the hearts of those purple roses…

And this poem ends with a repeating sentence: The sky is like blue satin! Has the poet ever written anything more vivid and novel than this? He believes not. He got some bold metaphors: "My heart is full of lilacs." He felt that there was an incredible dawn in his soul.

Naively, he asked himself uneasily, "But what's wrong with me? Am I going to get sick? I have a bit of cold and heat like before I had scarlet fever." But no, he feels happy! Happiness and misfortune are mixed together, he is simply confused; because his life before was so peaceful, so calm. Why does he tremble when her cherry lips reveal her snow-white teeth, smiling gracefully? Why is he eager to see her again? Three days ago, he did not know her at all. Before, he also loved his mother, his aunt, but he never had this feeling. For her, he is willing to give everything he has; yes, he has nothing, or almost nothing; apart from a beautiful annual gift book with illustrations of hummingbirds printed on it, he has nothing that she loves, but this beautiful book is hidden in the bookcase, and if he gives it to her, his aunt will be unhappy.

The day before yesterday he had thought about buying some rutabagas to send her, but undoubtedly, this must be a ridiculous act. And, opening his little purse, there were only six sous (Sou - one-twentieth of a franc), so he felt the sadness of poverty he had never felt before.
